44a4(phal chen): pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa dang smon lam la brtson pa'i yid rin po che yongs su dag pa grangs med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig /dbyangs rin po che rnam par
44a5(phal chen): dag pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pa'i dbyangs rin po che yongs su dag pa grangs med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ye shes rin po che sngon du 'gro ba'i lus kyi
44a6(phal chen): las rin po che grangs med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ye shes rin po che sgrib pa med pa la brtson pas ngag gi las rin po che yang dag par yongs su dag pa grangs med pa kun nas
44a7(phal chen): gnas par gyur cig / chags pa med pa'i ye shes rin po che'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las rin po che yangs shing yongs su dag par grangs med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig /sangs
44a8(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig dang yul gcig dang phyogs gcig dang / skra yi rtse mo re re zhing yang de ltar skye mched kyi ye shes rnam par dag pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
44b1(phal chen): tshad med pa nas byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i grangs dang bgrang ba las 'das pas kun tu gang bar gyur cig / phyogs gcig tu ji lta ba de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa
44b2(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad kyang yongs su gang bar gyur cig / de ltar byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag rin po che'i
44b3(phal chen): dmyigs pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag thams cad kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig bzung bas bsdus te spos rnam pa sna tshogs
44b4(phal chen): thams cad kyi spos kyi rgyal mtshan tshad med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / gzhung de ltar rin po che ji lta ba de bzhin du spos yongs su bsngo ba yang khong du chud par byas te/ ye shes kyi spos
44b5(phal chen): chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i spos kyi yid kyi las rgya chen po yongs su dag pa tshad med pa'i bar kun nas gnas par gyur cig / de bzhin du me tog sna tshogs thams cad kyi me tog
44b6(phal chen): gi brgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ces bya ba nas ye shes kyi me tog chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las me tog rgya che zhing yongs su dag pa
44b7(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / phreng ba dang byug pa sna tshogs thams cad kyi phreng ba dang byug pa'i rgyan mtshungs pa med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig /ces bya ba
44b8(phal chen): nas ye shes kyi phreng ba dang byug pa chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las kyi phreng ba dang byug pa'i rgyan rnam par dag pa mtshungs pa med pa'i bar du kun nas gnas par gyur cig / phye ma dang bdug pa sna tshogs thams cad kyi phye ma dang bdug pa'i brgyan sa mtshams med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig /
45a1(phal chen): ye shes kyi phye ma dang bdug pa chags pa med pa'i
45a2(phal chen): mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las kyi phye ma dang bdug pa yongs su dag pa sa mtshams med pa'i bar du kun nas gnas par gyur cig / gos dang chos gos thams cad kyi gos dang chos gos kyi
45a3(phal chen): brgyan mu med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ces bya ba nas ye shes kyi gos dang chos gos kyi brgyan chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las khrel yod pa dang / ngo tsha shes pa'i

45a5(phal chen): med pa kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ye shes kyi gdugs kyi brgyan chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yid kyi las ye shes kyis yang dag pa khyab pa yongs su dag pa sa mtshams

45b3(phal chen): kun nas gnas par gyur cig / ces bya ba nas nor bu rin po che thams cad kyi shing kun nas bres pa'i nor bu rin po che'i gdan rnam par dag pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa kun nas gnas par

45b5(phal chen): shes kyi nor bu rin po che rnam par dag pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du gnas par gyur cig ces/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos sbyin pa las stsogs
45b6(phal chen): pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyis bsgrub pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad yongs su dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir
45b7(phal chen): yongs su bsngo'o/ /sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid mi 'khrug pa yongs su dag pa dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo la 'jug pa dang / sems
45b8(phal chen): can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir bsod nams kyi stobs thub par rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir bsod nams kyi mtshan nyid rnam par dag pa zil

46a3(phal chen): dbyings kyis klas pa nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa shes par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyir sngon gyi mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam

46b8(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho re re zhing yang chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa'i ye shes kyi snang ba rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /tshig thams cad rab tu dbye bas shin tu bstan pa mngon par bsgrub bya
47a1(phal chen): yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir yongs su bsngo'o/ /chos 'byam klas pa mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad dang / chos kyi snang ba thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin rab tu thob par bya ba'i

49a7(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa nam mkha'i mthas gtugs pa thams cad yongs su dag pa thob par 'gyur ro/ /sems can

49b7(phal chen): mo dkrung gcig gis yongs su rgyas par byin gyis rlob kyang sems can thams cad la gnod pa med par 'gyur ro/ /dus gsum mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad la 'jug pa'i ye shes
49b8(phal chen): 'byam klas pa yongs su rdzogs par thob cing khong du chud par 'gyur ro/ /blo mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / chos
50a1(phal chen): thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / skye mched yongs su shes pa'i ye shes thams cad rnam par dag pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa thams cad la 'jug cing rgyas
50a2(phal chen): par 'gengs pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / sems can gyi ris dang skye gnas rnam pa sna tshogs su gyur pa thams cad nas byung ba'i sgra smra ba dang / bskod pa thams cad ma lus pa la mngon
50a3(phal chen): sum gyi ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par rnam pa mtha' yas pa'i 'od gzer dang / 'od kyi dkyil 'khor rab tu gtong zhing mtha' dang dbus med pa snang
50a4(phal chen): bar byed pa rnam par dag pa dang / dus gsum thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ma lus par mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da
50a5(phal chen): ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor mtha' dang dbus med pa ma lus pa thams cad la skad cig gcig tu 'jug pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa dang / sems can thams
50a6(phal chen): cad kyi mngon par 'du bya ba thams cad ma lus pa la 'jug pas 'gro ba mtha' dang dbus med pa rnam par dag par bya ba rab tu thob par 'gyur ro/ /yongs su rdzogs par byed do/ /
50a7(phal chen): rab tu bsgrub po/ /rnam par dag par byed do/ /mnyam par byed do/ /mngon sum du byed do/ /rab tu rtogs par byed do/ /khong du chud par byed do/ /yang dag par sems par byed do/ /rnam
50a8(phal chen): par dag pa thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa bya ba rjes su thob par byed do/ /de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs kyis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams su sangs rgyas
50b1(phal chen): kyi zhing brgya phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams rnam pa drug du g.yos te/ g.yos so/ /rab tu g.yos so/ /kun tu g.yos so/ /'gul to rab tu 'gul
50b2(phal chen): to/ /kun tu 'gul to/ /ldeg go rab tu ldeg to/ /kun tu ldeg go/ /chem chem rab tu chem chem/ kun tu chem chem mo/ /'ur 'ur rab tu 'ur 'ur/ kun tu 'ur 'ur ro/ /shig shig
50b3(phal chen): rab tu shig shig go/ /kun tu shig shig go/ /sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang chos nyid rab tu thob pas lha rdzas kyi me tog sprin gyi char yang mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi phreng ba'i sprin gyi char
50b4(phal chen): mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi phye ma'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi gos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi rin po che'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab
50b5(phal chen): po/ /lha rdzas kyi lhab lhub kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi spos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi nor bu rin po che'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /
50b6(phal chen): lha rdzas kyi dus dang mthun pa'i tsan dan gyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi sbrul gyi snying po'i tsan dan mchog gi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi gdugs dang
50b7(phal chen): rgyal mtshan dang ba dan kha dog sna tshogs kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi lha'i lus grangs med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi dbyangs
50b8(phal chen): kyi yan lag brjod du med pa'i tshig dang brjod pa la rtogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong bar spyod pa'i chos rin po che'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas
51a1(phal chen): kyi de bzhin gshegs pas bstod pa'i sangs rgyas kyi bsngags pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi legs so zhes bya ba dang / lhung lhung 'degs
51a2(phal chen): kyi sgra 'byin pa dang / dga' bar byed pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po/ /lha rdzas kyi lha'i bu lus bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med cing brjod du med pas rab tu
51a3(phal chen): btud do/ /lha yul gyi lha'i bu grangs med pa sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa la brtson par yid la byed cing / de bzhin gshegs pa la shin tu dad pa'i sems kyi rgyud dang ldan pa/
51a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang mi 'bral ba'i sems kyis mngon par gnas so/ /lha rdzas kyi rol mo brdung ba dang bkrol ba'i sgra dang / lha'i glu'i dbyangs kyi tshul grangs med

51a8(phal chen): b zhi pa 'di dga' ldan gyi gnas su lha'i dbang po rab dga' ldan gyi khang pa na ji lta ba bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du yang phyogs bcur brgyas par bkang zhing chos bstan
51b1(phal chen): pa 'di nyid kun tu byung ngo / /sangs rgyas kyi mthus phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi pha rol dag nas kyang sangs rgyas kyi
51b2(phal chen): zhing brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' lhags nas phyogs bcu bkang ste/ 'di skad zer to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar khyod kyis yongasu bsngo ba'i

51b7(phal chen): snyed kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams phyin pa mngon du mthong ba sha stag sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs gyis 'khor 'dir phyin to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i
51b8(phal chen): rgyal mtshan gyi phyogs bcur ltas te 'khor thams cad la bltas te chos kyi dbyings la rnam par blta ba dang / don dang tshig dang yi ge la rab tu 'jug pa dang / sems bskyed pa mtha'
52a1(phal chen): dang dbus med par yangs pa yongs su bsgoms pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad la snying rje chen pos khyab par bya ba dang / dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs su sems yang dag

56a1(phal chen): yul rgyas par 'gengs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan dang nan tan yongs su rdzogs pa thams cad bskal pa brjod du myed par yang dag par bstan pa la nan tan
56a2(phal chen): bsngags shing brjod pa zad myi shes pa sha stag ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po
56a3(phal chen): che'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpe' sems dpa' chen po pad mo'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems
56a4(phal chen): dpa' chen po pad mo dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nyi ma'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gtsang ba'i snying po dang /
56a5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po zla ba dri ma myed pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen
56a6(phal chen): po brgyan rnam par bkod pa thams cad rab tu snang bar ston pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ye shes rnam par snang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems
56a7(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal yid du 'ong ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tsan dan dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
56a8(phal chen): chen po me tog dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po me tog rgyas pa dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal
56b1(phal chen): lha'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bsod nams dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sgrib pa myed pa'i ye shes rnam par
56b2(phal chen): dag pa'i dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mthu chen dpal gyi
56b3(phal chen): snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dri ma myed pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dri ma dang bral ba'i snying po dang / byang chub
56b4(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po spos sna tshogs brgyan gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'od gzer gyi dra ba chen po rab tu snang ba'i snying po dang /
56b5(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'od dri ma myed pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid bzang po'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gser bzang zhing
56b6(phal chen): dri ma myed pa'i dbyig gis spras pa'i gzi brjid mdzes pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mtshan thams cad kyis brgyan pas rnam par dag pa'i
56b7(phal chen): dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dpal gyi bi'u rdo rje 'od 'phro bas brgyan pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
56b8(phal chen): 'od 'bar zhing 'phro ba'i dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po skar ma'i rgyal po 'od 'phro rab tu snang ba'i snying po dang / byang chub sems
57a1(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha' mdzod ye shes sgrib pa myed pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor sgrib
57a2(phal chen): pa myed cing nga ro snyan pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gzungs kyi snying po yon tan gyi 'gro ba thams cad kyi smon lam thams cad yang dag par 'dzin
57a3(phal chen): pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rgya mtsho brgyan gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ri rab dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems
57a4(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po yon tan thams cad rnam par dag pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po dang / byang chub sems
57a5(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas dpal gyi snying po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam par grol ba'i zla ba dang / de dag la stsogs pa byang chub
57a6(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshad med pa gzhal du myed pa/ grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ mtshungs pa myed pa dpag tu myed pa/ kun tu mtha' yas pa
57a7(phal chen): dang mu myed pa sa mtshams myed pa/ brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du med pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po la stsogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing sna tshogs nas 'dus
57a8(phal chen): pa sha stag dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs so/ /de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po sangs rgyas kyi mthus theg pa chen po rab tu snang
57b1(phal chen): ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la bsnyoms par zhugs so/ /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin theg pa chen po rab tu snang ba de la mnyam par bzhag
57b2(phal chen): ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyis phyogs re re'i 'jig rten gyis khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi pha rol nas/ sangs rgyas bcom
57b3(phal chen): ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun kyang mtshan rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar 'thun pa sha stag gis zhal mngon par bstan te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
57b4(phal chen): de dag gis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to/ /rigs kyi bu de ltar khyod byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin theg pa chen po rab tu snang ba la snyoms par zhugs pa legs so legs so/ /
57b5(phal chen): 'di ltar rigs kyi bu khyod la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kun mtshan rdo rje'i snying po zhes bya bar mthun
57b6(phal chen): pa sha stag gis/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad 'di'i sngon gyi smon lam gyi byin gyis
57b7(phal chen): brlabs dang / khyod nyid kyi ye shes khyad par gyis byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi chos snang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu brjod cing ye shes kyi sa la 'jug
57b8(phal chen): par bya ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsdu ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rab tu dbye bar bya ba dang / chos thams cad la ye shes shin tu yangs par
58a1(phal chen): bya ba dang / shin tu legs par gnas pa'i chos rab tu bstan pa dang / ye shes tha myi dad pa rnam par sbyang ba dang 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad kyis gos pa myed par bya ba dang / 'jig
58a2(phal chen): rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dag par bya ba dang / ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul khong du chud par bya ba nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul gyi bar du khong du chud par bya
58a3(phal chen): ba dang / 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa bcu brtsams pa rab tu thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sa ma nor bar mngon par rnam par bgod pa shin tu bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
58a4(phal chen): thams cad la yang dag par dmyigs par bya ba dang / zag pa myed pa'i chos kyi bye brag rnam par bsgom pa dang / rnam par dbye ba shin tu rnam par phye ba'i shes rab kyi snang ba chen po la
58a5(phal chen): mkhas pa'i ye shes kyi rgyan thob par bya ba dang / shin tu brtags pa'i ye shes kyi sgo la 'jug par bya ba dang / gnas kyi rnam pa ci rigs su brjod pa dang / spobs pa'i snang ba
58a6(phal chen): dma' ba myed pa thob par bya ba dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa chen po'i sa shin tu rtogs par bya ba dang / byang chub kyi sems dran pa nyams pa myed par bya ba dang / sems
58a7(phal chen): can gyi khams thams cad yongs su smyin par bya ba dang / thams cad du song ba'i blo rnam par gdon myi za ba la mkhas pa rab tu thob par bya ba'i phyir byin gyis brlab pa mdzad do/ /
58a8(phal chen): de bas na rigs kyi bu khyod kyis chos kyi sgo rab tu dbye ba la mkhas par 'gyur ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes
58b1(phal chen): snang ba'i byin gyis brlabs kyis rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dag par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings shin tu sbyangs pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad la phan gdags
58b2(phal chen): pa dang / chos kyi sku'i ye shes kyi lus la 'jug par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyis dbang bskur ba yang dag par blang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams
58b3(phal chen): cad du shin tu 'phags pa'i lus 'byung bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi lam gyi rgyud thams cad las yang dag par 'da' bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyi
58b4(phal chen): tshul yongs su dag par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir spobs pa bskyed cig /de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de
58b5(phal chen): dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po zil gyis myi non par lus nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /thogs pa myed pa'i spobs pas shin tu ston pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /
58b6(phal chen): shin tu sbyangs pa'i ye shes rnam par phye ba la 'jug pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /dran pa nyams pa myed pa'i byin gyis brlab nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /shin tu nges par rtogs pas
58b7(phal chen): mkhas pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i blo'i rjes su 'gro ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi stobs thub pa myed
58b8(phal chen): pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i myi 'jigs pa che zhing zhum pa myed pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang tha dad par
59a1(phal chen): mdzad pa mkhyen pas rnam par dbye ba'i chos kyi tshul shin tu rtogs pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyan shin tu rnam par phye ba mngon par
59a2(phal chen): bsdu ba nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni ting nge 'dzin de nyid kyi chos nyid rab tu thob pa dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis nye bar bsgrub pa dang / lhag pa'i
59a3(phal chen): bsam pa shin tu rnam par sbyangs pa dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor shin tu sbyangs pa dang / tshogs shin tu bstsags pa dang / yongs su sbyang ba shin tu byas pa dang / dran
59a4(phal chen): pa'i snod tshad med pa dang / mos pa rnam par dag cing 'od shin tu gsal ba dang / gzungs kyi sgo tha mi dad pa thob pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgyas
59a5(phal chen): shin tu btab pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis de dag na bzhugs bzhin du rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus so so nas phyag g.yas pa brkyang ste/
59a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po'i mgo la byug pa mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la reg ma thag tu de nyid kyi tshe ting nge
59a7(phal chen): 'dzin de las langs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /des na byang chub sems dpa'i smon lam 'di ni shin tu rnam par gdon mi za ste/
59a8(phal chen): tha mi dad pa ltar med pa chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par yangs pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad dang /
59b1(phal chen): sems can gyi khams thams cad rgyas par khyab pa/ 'gro ba thams cad yongs su skyob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa ste/ kye rgyal
59b2(phal chen): ba'i sras dag de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ro/ /ma byon
59b3(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu 'jug par 'gyur ro/ /da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa la yang rab tu
59b4(phal chen): 'jug par 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de la bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi sa rnams te/ gang la bsams te bdag gis de skad du smras pa
59b5(phal chen): de dag ni 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so/ /gsung ngo / /gsung bar 'gyur ro/ /bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/
59b6(phal chen): rab tu dga' ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po dang / dri ma dang bral ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa gnyis pa dang / 'od byed pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa
59b7(phal chen): gsum pa dang / 'od 'phro ba can zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa bzhi pa dang / rgyal bar dka' ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa dang / mngon gsum tu byed pa zhes bya ba
59b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i sa drug pa dang / sa ring du song ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa dang / mi g.yo ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad pa dang / legs pa'i
60a1(phal chen): blo gros zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa dgu pa dang / chos kyi sprin ces bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems
60a2(phal chen): dpa'i sa bcu pa ste/ de ni 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis gsungs so/ /gsung ngo / /gsung bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /bdag gis ni sangs
60a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing gang na 'ang de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po 'di dag mi gsung ba de lta bu ma mthong ngo / /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /
60a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i lam yongs su sbyong ba'i chos snang ba'i sgo 'di ni yang dag phul zhes bya ba yin te/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa rnam par dgod pa
60a5(phal chen): shin tu bstan pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag gnas 'di ni bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes pa'o/ /de nas de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems
60a6(phal chen): dpa'i sa bcu 'di dag ming tsam zhig brjod de cang mi zer bar 'dug nas/ de las rab tu phye ste ma bshad pa dang / de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag thams cad byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu po 'di dag ming tsam
60a7(phal chen): zhig thos la rab tu phye ste/ mi brjod pas skom par gyur nas de dag 'di snyam du sems te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu de dag ming tsam zhig brjod cing cang mi
60a8(phal chen): zer bar 'dug nas/ de las rab tu phye zhing mi ston pa de la rgyu ni gang rkyen ni ci zhig yod snyam pa dang / de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor 'dus pa de na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnam
60b1(phal chen): par grol ba'i zla ba zhes bya ba 'dus shing 'dug 'dug ste/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag gi sems kyi yongs su rtog pa sems kyis yongs su
60b2(phal chen): shes nas/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la glu'i dbyangs kyis tshig gis tshigs su bcad de don de dris so/ /ci phyir rtog pa rnam dag cing / /dran dang ye shes ldan pa yis/ /sa yi mchog ni brjod byas te/ /
60b3(phal chen): mkhas pas rnam par phye myi bshad/ /'di kun nges par rtogs pa ste/ /byang chub sems dpa' grags chen yin/ /ci phyir khyod kyi sa brjod de/ /rab tu bye ba bshad mi bgyi/ /rgyal sras 'jigs med 'di dag ni/ /kun kyang shin tu nyan par 'dod/ /
60b4(phal chen): sa yi don tshul yang dag tu/ /rnam par phye ste bshad par mdzod/ /'khor 'di shin tu rnam dang ste/ /le lo med cing dge dang ldan/ /dag pa'i mchog la gnas pa ste/ /
60b5(phal chen): yon tan ye shes ldan pa yi/ /phan tshun gcig la gcig lta zhing / /kun kyang rim gro bcas par gnas/ /sbrang rtsi ji ltar spang myin pa/ /de ltar bdud rtsi mchog kyang 'dod/ /rdo rje snying po 'jigs myed pa/ /
60b6(phal chen): shes rab chen pos de thos nas/ /'khor rnams dga' bar bya ba'i phyir/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i sras la smras/ /sangs rgyas sku rab yang dag 'byung bas na/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rab bstan
60b7(phal chen): cing / /sa rgyu dam pa rnam par dbye bya ba/ /de ni rmad 'byung mchog tu dga' ba yin/ /phra zhing blta dka' rnam par rtog pa spangs/ /sems kyi sa dang bral bas bsgrub dka'/ /mkhas pa
60b8(phal chen): rnams kyi zag med spyod yul te/ /'gro ba rnams kyis de thos mos par 'gyur/ /rdo rje lta bur bsam pa rab gzhag ste/ /sangs rgyas ye shes mchog la mos byas shing / /bdag med pa yi
60b9(phal chen): sems kyi sa shes na/ /ye shes dam pa 'di bzod nyan par nus/ /ji ltar bar snang 'ja' mtshon bris pa dang / /nam mkha'i dbyings la rlung gnas ji bzhin du/ /de ltar ye shes zag pa med pa yang / /
61a1(phal chen): shin tu blta dka' thub pas rnam par phye/ /de la bdag gis sems ni 'di snyam byed/ /sangs rgyas ye shes dam pa bsam yas la/ /'gro ba gang rnams smra bar byed dkon zhes/ /
61a2(phal chen): de yi phyir na ma smras ma bshad do/ /de skad smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la 'di skad smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'di ni byang chub
61a3(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos 'di dag bsam pa shin tu sbyangs pa kun tu rtog pa/ yon yongs su sbyangs pa spyad par bya ba shin tu spyod/ tshogs shin tu bstsags pa/ sangs rgyas bye ba brgya stong shin tu
61a4(phal chen): bsnyen bkur ba/ yon tan dang ye shes tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ the tsom dang nem nur med pa/ nyon mongs pa dang bral ba/ mos pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pa la rab tu gnas pa/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa sha
61a5(phal chen): stag tshogs pas yongs su dag pa yin gyis/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis legs par bshad pa mdzod cig dang / byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad ni rnam pa 'di lta bu'i gnas zab
61a6(phal chen): mo la mngon sum du gnas pa sha stag go/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas don 'di nyid gsal bar bslab pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la tshigs su bcad de
61a7(phal chen): smras pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bla na med/ /sa rnams rab phye rnams dgod brtags pa yi/ /ye shes sbyongs zhing byang chub thob byed pa/ /mchog dang dam pa zhi ba'i chos rnams shod/ /'khor
61a8(phal chen): 'di dag pa nyon mongs med pa'i mchog / mos dang bsam pa shin tu sbyangs pa ste/ /sangs rgyas bye ba mang la spyad pa spyod/ /sa 'di brtag la yod ces ldan pa yin/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa'
61b1(phal chen): rdo rje'i snying pos byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla ba la 'di skad ces smras so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po chos kyi rnam pa 'di lta bu'i gnas
61b2(phal chen): zab mo la sbyangs pa/ kun tu rtog pa yongs su sbyangs pa/ spyod pa shin tu spyad pa/ tshogs shin tu bstsags pa/ sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong la dge ba'i rtsa ba shin tu bstsags pa/ yon tan dang ye
61b3(phal chen): shes tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ the tsom dang ner nur med pa/ nyon mongs pa dang bral ba/ mos pa dang lhag pa'i bsam pa la rab tu gnas pa/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa sha stag pas shin tu dag pa yang yin
61b4(phal chen): na/ 'on kyang sems can mos pa chung gzhan dag gis zab mo'i rnam pa 'di lta bu bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas dag thos par gyur la thos nas kyang the tsom dang yid gnyis su gyur na de dag la yun ring por smod
61b5(phal chen): pa dang / don myed pa dang / mi bde ba'i rgyur 'gyur bas 'di lta zhig tu snying brtse ba'i phyir bdag ni cang mi zer bar 'dug pa nyid du mos so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos don 'di
61b6(phal chen): nyid gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /'khor 'di rnam dag shes rab yangs pa ste/ /zab cing gsal ba'i spyod ldan rtogs shes shing / /gzhan gyi dring 'jog ri rgyal
61b7(phal chen): bzhin mi g.yo/ /bsam rtog mi 'khrug rgya mtsho chen po 'dra/ /'on kyang mi rtogs mi shes ma spyad pa/ /rnam shes yul nas don la shes med pas/ thos shing ma ches phral du ngan song
61b8(phal chen): ltung / /de dag snying brtses ye shes sa ma bshad/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas yang byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la gsol ba btab pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
62a1(phal chen): legs par bshad pa mdzod gcig dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis rnam pa 'di lta bu bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i gnas 'di dag kyang gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / legs par yid ches par
62a2(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de ni 'di ltar sa shin tu bstan pa 'di bshad pa'i tshe chos nyid rab tu thob/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis kyang dgongs par 'gyur ro/ /byang chub sems
62a3(phal chen): dpa' thams cad kyang ye shes kyi sa 'di yongs su bsrung ba'i don du rab tu brtson par byed do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ni spyod pa'i dang po ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par 'grub
62a4(phal chen): pa'i gzhi yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ yi ge dang 'bru dang bgrang ba ji snyed du bstan pa de dag thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro ba'ang yi ge'i phyi mo'o/ /tha mar yang yi ge'i phyi mo
62a5(phal chen): la thug ste/ yi ge'i phyi mo bstan pas ma khyab pa de lta bu'i yi ge dang 'bru bgrang ba bstan pa ni gang yang med do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang spyod pas rab
62a6(phal chen): tu 'grub pa sngon du 'gro'o/ /rang byung gi ye shes kyi mthar thug par 'gyur bas/ sa'i mthar thug pa med do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras shod gcig dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
62a7(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyang yongs su bsrung ba'i phyir byin gyis brlob pa mdzad do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas don 'di nyid gsal bar brjod pa bslab pa'i
62a8(phal chen): phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ sa dang spyod 'jug byang chub sems 'gyur ye shes bsgrub byed pa/ /spyod pa rnam dag thams cad mkhyen
62b1(phal chen): pa'i sras kyis legs par shod/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba bde gshegs kun mgon 'den pa ji snyed pa/ /khyu mchog de kun ye shes 'byung gnas ston la dgongs pa mdzad/ /'di ni dang po zhugs pa'i
62b2(phal chen): shes spyod 'di mthar thug ste/ /rgyal ba'i chos rab gzhal yas ji snyed de dag 'byung gnas 'di/ /yi ge bgrang ba phyi ma'i rjes 'gro sngon du 'gro ba ltar/ /de bzhin dus mchog blo yi yul du tha ma
62b3(phal chen): thug par 'dod/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' de dag thams cad gyi dbyangs kyi nga ro gcig tu glu'i dbyangs kyis tshigs su bcad de/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying po la don 'di nyid kyi phyir/
62b4(phal chen): gsol ba btab pa/ blo yangs dam pa'i phul mnga' ba/ /spobs pa mtha' yas rnam par dbye ba rtogs mkhyen pas/ /yid du 'ong ba'i gsung dbyangs kyis/ /'gro la phan don dam pa bshad par
62b5(phal chen): mdzod/ /dran dang dga' bas spyod dag pa/ /stobs bcu'i stobs kyis shugs stsogs yon tan ldan pa yi/ /sa yi dam pa mchog gis rnams/ /tha dad yang dag don mkhyen spyod pas shod/ /zhi sdom
62b6(phal chen): bsgrub pa'i yid ldan pa/ /nga rgyal dregs dang lta ba'i nyon mongs zhir gyur pas/ /'khor 'dir the rtsom bral ba ste/ /khyod kyis legs par bshad do re zhig sdod/ /skom pa bsil ba'i chu 'dod bzhin/ /
62b7(phal chen): bkres pa kha zas nad pa sman rab 'dod pa dang / /bung ba sbrang rtsi 'dod pa ltar/ /de bzhin 'khor 'di khyod kyi tshig la sdod/ /de bas shin tu blo yangs pas/ /rdul med rnams la sa yi dam pa 'jug par
62b8(phal chen): shod/ /chags med stobs bcu'i tshogs gyur pa/ /bde gshegs spyod pa ma lus bshad par mdzod/ /de nas de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das shakya thub pa'i mdzod spu nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i stobs
63a1(phal chen): snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer gyi 'khor gyi 'od gzer brgya stong grangs med pa dang ldan pa byung ngo / /de byung nas phyogs bcu thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar
63a2(phal chen): byas nas/ sems can thams cad kyi ngan song gi sdug bsngal thams cad rtsi zil bar byas ste/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor
63a3(phal chen): snang bar byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi rnam pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i mthu bstan nas phyogs bcu thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor
63a4(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor du chos bstan pa'i byin gyis rlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i lus snang bar byas ste/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba bsam gyis myi khyab pa bstan nas/ steng gi bar snang la 'od gzer
63a5(phal chen): stug po'i sprin gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen por byas te 'dug go/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi mdzod spu dag nas kyang byang chub sems dpa'i 'od snang ba zhes bya ba'i 'od gzer gyi 'khor
63a6(phal chen): gyi 'od gzer grangs myed pa byung bar gyur to/ /byung nas kyang de dag gis phyogs bcu thams cad du 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa kun tu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du chos bstan
63a7(phal chen): pa'i byin gyis brlabs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams snang bar byas te sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams mi 'jed 'di yang snang bar byas te/
63a8(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor 'di 'ang snang bar byas ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje'i snying po'i lus snang bar byas nas/ steng gi
63b1(phal chen): bar snang la de bzhin du 'od gzer stug po'i sprin gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen por byas te 'khod do/ /de nas 'od gzer stug po'i sprin gyi dra ba'i khang pa brtsegs pa chen po de dag nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis sgra'i
63b2(phal chen): rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ngo / /mi mnyam mnyam dang mnyam pa mkha' dang mnyam pa dag /stobs bcu'i khyu mchog mthu ldan tshad med yon tan can/ /'jig rten kun mchog myi yi dam pa phul gyi rnams/ /shAkya
63b3(phal chen): seng ge'i chos la byin brlabs dam pa mdzad/ /bde gshegs sras po 'dren pa'i byin gyis bshad par bgyis/ /chos rgyal khyu mchog rnams kyi mdzod kyi dam pa phye/ /sa yi ye shes rnam phye spyod mchog rab
63b4(phal chen): yangs pa/ /stobs bcu'i byin gyis ma thogs myur du bstan pa gyis/ /gang gi rna lam bsam par chos dam rin chen 'di/ /song bar gyur pa de dag bde gshegs byin gyis rlabs/ /rdul med sa kun rim gyis
63b5(phal chen): rab tu rdzogs byas nas/ /stobs bcu ldan pa'i rgyal ba dam par 'grub par 'gyur/ /rgya mtsho'i chu byung gyur cing skal pa'i myes gdungs kyang / /gal te snod gyur sems can de dag 'di la nyan/ /gang rnams
63b6(phal chen): the tsom za zhing yid gnyis byed pa na/ /de dag rna bas rnam pa kun tu thos mi 'gyur/ /de phyir sa yi ye shes lam mchog bstan par bgyis/ /gnas dang rgyud dang 'phro ba rim gyis rab tu shod/ /spyod dang yul
63b7(phal chen): dang chos dang ye shes tshul rnams kyi/ /chos kyi tshul yang 'gro ba kun la phan phyir shod/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos phyogs bcur bltas nas/ 'khor thams cad de bas kyang dad par bya
63b8(phal chen): ba'i phyir de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so/ /phra la shes dga' drang srong chen po'i lam/ /mi rtog rtog yul ma yin lta bar dka'/ /rang bzhin zhi zhing 'gag med 'byung ba med/ /mkhas
64a1(phal chen): gsal shes pas khong du chud pa yin/ /ngo bo nyid stong zhi zhing sdug bsngal zad/ /rgyud las rnam grol mnyam par mya ngan 'das/ /mtha' dang dbus med tshig gis brjod du med/ /dus gsum
64a2(phal chen): grol ba nam mkha' 'dra zhing mtshungs/ /bde gshegs spyod yul zhi zhing nye bar zhi/ /smra ba'i lam rnams kun gyis brjod par dka'/ /de dag sa dang spyod pa de 'dra ba/ /smra bar dka' na bstan par ga la
64a3(phal chen): nus/ /de ni bsam yas sems lam rnam par spangs/ /ye shes rnam par bsgrub pa rgyal ba'i spyod yul te/ /phung po skye mched khams kyi bskyed byed min/ /sems kyis mi shes yid kyis rnam ma
64a4(phal chen): brtags/ /ji ltar bar snang gnas kyi bya yi rjes/ /shin tu smra dka' bstan par mi nus pa/ /de ltar bde gshegs sras kyi sa rnams kyang / /yid dang sems kyi yul gyis shes mi nus/ /'on kyang
64a5(phal chen): byams dang snying rje smon lam gyis/ /de las phyogs tsam rim pa'i tshul bzhin du/ /bshad par bya ste sems kyi spyod yul min/ /yul gyi ye shes tshul gyis rdzogs par bya ba'o/ /de 'dra'i spyod yul
64a6(phal chen): phra zhing blta dka' ba/ /rang rig yin pas brjod par mi nus kyang / /'on kyang bde bar gshegs pa'i mthus brjod kyis/ /thams cad mthun par nan tan gyis de nyon/ /ye shes sa dang spyod 'jug ci 'dra ba/ /
64a7(phal chen): bskal pa bye bar zad par mi nus te/ /yang dag don dngos gzhan min gnas pa las/ /mdo tsam bshad kyis de dag mnyan par gyis/ /'thun zhing nan tan yod par sta gon gnos/ /bde gshegs byin gyis
64a8(phal chen): bdag gis bshad par bya/ /dpe ldan 'thad la yi ge mnyam pa yi/ /chos sgra dam pa bdag gis brjod par bya/ /'di ni tshig gis brjod par shin tu dka'/ /de ltar tshad med bde gshegs mthu dag las/ /
64b1(phal chen): chu thigs gcig 'dra bdag gi lus 'di la/ /de ring zhugs kyi bshad pa mnyan par gyis/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems can dge ba'i rtsa ba shin tu bstsags pa shin tu gcod pa/ tshogs shin tu bstsags pa/
64b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'byung ba shin tu bsnyen bkur ba/ chos dkar po shin tu bsdus pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis shin tu bzung ba/ bsam pa yongs su dag pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa shin tu rgya chen po can mos pa
64b3(phal chen): rgya chen po dang ldan pa/ snying rje dang snying brtse ba can mngon du gyur pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la mngon par mos pa rnams rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mos pa dang / stobs bcu'i stobs thob par bya

65a1(phal chen): shes kyi man ngag yang dag par tshol ba/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad las gdams ngag yang dag par blang ba/ chos kyi dbyings kyi klas pa/ nam mkha'i mthar thugs par gnas pa/

66b8(phal chen): k yi sems myi bsgul ba dang 'jig rten gyi bya ba thams cad la mngon par dga' ba myed pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i lam dang ldan pa dang mi ngoms par byang chub kyi yan lag gi
67a1(phal chen): t shogs rab tu bstsogs pa dang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par gong nas gong du khyad par du 'phags pa'i lam tshol ba dang sa yongs su sbyong ba'i chos kyi rnam pa 'di lta bu dag dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems
67a2(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba la gnas pa yin te/ de byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba de la gnas shing rnam pa 'di lta bu'i smon lam chen po dang /
67a3(phal chen): nor brtson pa chen po dang / mngon par bsgrub pa chen po 'di dag mngon par bsgrub ste/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas thams cad ma lus pa lhag ma myed par mtha' dang dbus mchod rim gro bya ba'i phyir rnam pa'i
67a4(phal chen): mchog thams cad dang ldan pa mos pa rgya chen pos rnam par dag pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ bskal pa grangs med pa thams cad du sangs
67a5(phal chen): rgyas skyes pa bgrangs pa la rim gro dang mchod pa chen po rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub bo/ /'di lta ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa'i chos kyi tshul
67a6(phal chen): yang dag par gzung ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub yang dag par blang pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par bsrung ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings
67a7(phal chen): kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mur thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba bgrangs pa'i chos dam pa'i chos yongs su
67a8(phal chen): gzung ba rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi pho brang
67b1(phal chen): dam pa na bzhugs pa la stsogs te/ 'pho ba dang gshegs pa dang / sku ni bzhugs pa dang / skye ba dang / gzhon nur rol pa dang / btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa dang / mngon par 'byung ba dang /
67b2(phal chen): bka' ba spyad pa dang / snying po byang chub tu gshegs pa dang / bdud gdul ba dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gsol ba gdab pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor ba dang / mya ngan las 'das
67b3(phal chen): pa chen po ston pa'i drung du 'gro zhing mchod pa dang / rim gro bya ba dang / dam pa'i chos yang dag par gzung ba'i sbyor ba las stsogs pa thams cad gcig tu mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings
67b4(phal chen): kyis klas par rgya che ba nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa grangs med par thams cad du sangs rgyas 'byung ba bgrangs pa'i drung du 'gro ba nas/ mya ngan las 'das pa chen
67b5(phal chen): po'i bar gyi drung du 'gro ba rgyun mi chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya chen po shin tu yangs pa tshad med pa/ mi 'phrogs pa tha mi dad pa pha rol
67b6(phal chen): tu phyin pa thams cad kyis yang dag par bsdus pa/ sa yongs su sbyang ba'i yan lag dang nye ba'i yan lag du bcas pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / mtshan nyid dang bye brag gi mtshan nyid du bcas pa dang /
67b7(phal chen): 'grub pa dang 'jig pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod par gtogs pa thams cad dang / sa ji lta ba bzhin dang / ji lta bur bstan pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su sbyang ba la gdams ngag dang /
67b8(phal chen): man ngag gi sbyin pa nye bar bstan pa'i sems bskyed pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i 'tha'i mur thug pa/
68a1(phal chen): bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du spyod pa bgrangs pa sems bskyed pas mngon par bsgrub pa/ rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ sems can kyi khams
68a2(phal chen): thams cad ma lus pa lhag ma myed pa mtha' dag gzugs yod pa/ gzugs myed pa dang / 'du shes yod pa dang / 'du shes med pa dang / 'du shes yod pa'ang ma yin/ 'du shes med pa 'ang ma yin/
68a3(phal chen): sgo nga las skyes pa dang / mngal las skyes pa dang / drod gsher las skyes pa dang / rdzus te byung ba khams gsum du gtogs pa/ 'gro ba drug tu 'dus pa/ skye ba thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can
68a4(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba sangs rgyas kyi chos la bzung ba dang / lam gyi rgyud bgrangs pa thams cad rgyun gcod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la dgod pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings
68a5(phal chen): kyis klas par/ rgya che ba nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad dang / sems can bgrangs pa thams cad du sems can gyi khams yongs
68a6(phal chen): su smin par bya ba rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub bo/ /'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams yangs pa dang / dog pa dang / rgya chen po dang / tshad myed pa dang / phra ba dang / che ba dang / snrel
68a7(phal chen): gzhi dang / spyi'u tshugs rgyu ba thams cad ma lus pa lhag ma myed pa mtha' dag gzhi mnyam par yang dag par 'jug pa khong du chud par bya ba dang / myig 'phrul gyi rnam pa ltar phyogs bcu'i rnam pa tha dad
68a8(phal chen): ma lus pa'i rnam pa la 'jug pa/ rnam par phye ba'i ye shes khong du chud cing / mngon du 'gyur bar bya ba'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i
68b1(phal chen): mur thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad la 'jug cing yongs su dag par bya ba'i phyir smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ zhing thams cad zhing gcig tu
68b2(phal chen): yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / zhing gcig zhing thams cad du yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / yongs su sbyang ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med pa 'od mang po'i rgyan gyis rab tu brgyan par bya ba dang /
68b3(phal chen): kun nas nyon mongs pa thams cad bstsal bas/ yongs su dag pa'i lam dang ldan pa dang / sems can ye shes kyi 'byung gnas tshad med pas yongs su gang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi yul rgya chen po la
68b4(phal chen): yang dag par gzhol zhing khong du chud par bya ba dang / bsam pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can rnams la yang dag par bstan cing shin tu tshim par bya ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par/ rgya che ba
68b5(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mthar thug pa mur thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du zhing bgrangs par sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag par bya ba la rgyun mi 'chad pa'i
68b6(phal chen): smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad dang bsam pa gcig pa'i sbyor ba dang / lhod pa myed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad brtsal ba dang / byang
68b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa' thams cad dmyigs pa gcig cing mnyam pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par 'grogs shing mi 'bral ba dang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba ci dgar bstan
68b8(phal chen): pa dang / rang gi sems bskyed pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yul dang / mthu dang ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / ma nyams shing rjes su 'brang ba'i mngon par shes pa rab
69a1(phal chen): tu thob par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyis khams thams cad du rnam par rgyu bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du gzugs brnyan 'byung ba yang dag par bstan pa
69a2(phal chen): dang / skye ba'i skye gnas thams cad du rang gi lus rjes su 'gro bar bya ba dang / theg pa chen po bsam gyis myi khyab pa dang ldan pa'i/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun myi 'chad pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings
69a3(phal chen): kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i 'thar thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du spyod pa/ bgrangs par theg pa chen po mngon par bsgrub pa la rgyun
69a4(phal chen): myi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo la yang dag par gnas shing byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa spyad pa dang / lus dang / ngag dang yid kyi
69a5(phal chen): las don yod par bya ba dang / mthong ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi chos gdon mi za bar 'thob par bya ba dang / dbyangs brjod ma thag tu ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / dad par gyur ma thag tu
69a6(phal chen): nyon mongs pa phyir mi ldog par bya ba dang / bsam pa smen gyi rgyal po lta bu rab tu thob par bya ba dang / lus yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu 'thob par bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad
69a7(phal chen): spyad pa'i phyir chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du phyir myi ldog pa'i 'khor
69a8(phal chen): lo grangs par spyod pa thams cad du 'bras bu yod pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub po/ /'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bla na myed pa yang dag par rdzogs
69b1(phal chen): pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / skra'i sbubs gcig dang tha mi dad pa'i skra'i sbubs thams cad du tshe dang skye ba dang / gzhon nu rol pa dang / btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa dang / mngon
69b2(phal chen): par byung ba dang rnam par 'phrul pa dang snying po byang chub tu gshegs pa dang / bdud 'dul ba dang mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / gsol ba gdab pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo chen po bskor ba dang / yongs
69b3(phal chen): su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yul dang mthu dang ye shes chen po khong du chud par bya ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du sangs
69b4(phal chen): rgyas 'byung ba dang / skad cig gcig tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / rab tu zhi ba thob par bya ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya ba gcig gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'phrul
69b5(phal chen): pas rgyas par dgang ba dang / dbyangs gcig brjod pas sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi sems dang / bsam pa shin tu tshim par bya ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa chen po yongs su
69b6(phal chen): bstan pa dang / spyod pa rnams rgyun mi 'chad par bya ba dang / theg pa chen po'i sa la chos thams cad rnam par dgod pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / chos shes pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi rgyu dang / mngon
69b7(phal chen): par shes pa dang dbang gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad sprul pas rnam par bgang ba'i phyir/ chos kyi dbyings kyis klas par rgya che ba/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa/ phyi ma'i mtha'i
69b8(phal chen): mur thug pa/ bskal pa bgrangs pa thams cad du mngon par 'tshang rgya ba bgrangs par ye shes chen po'i mngon par shes pa rgyun mi 'chad pa'i smon lam chen po mngon par bsgrub bo/ /kye rgyal ba'i

70a2(phal chen): lam brgya stong grangs med pa phrag bcu tshang ba dag / byang chub sems dpa'i sa rab tu dga' ba la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpas thob po/ /mngon par bsgrub po/ /smon lam de dag kyang mthar
70a3(phal chen): thug pa'i gnas bcus mngon par bsgrub ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sems can gyi khams kyi mthar thug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mthar thug pa dang / nam mkha'i khams

70a7(phal chen): po 'di dag sems can gyi mthar mthar thug pa de'i mthar thug par gyur cig / smon lam chen po 'di dag 'jig rten gyi khams kyi mtha' gang du thug pa dang / nam mkha'i khams dang chos kyi khams

70b1(phal chen): rten gyi rgyud dang / chos kyi rgyud dang / ye shes kyi rgyud kyi khams kyi 'tha' gang du thug pa/ de'i mthar thug par gyur gcig /ji ltar sems can gyi khams mthar thug pa med pa dang / 'jig rten

70b4(phal chen): du smon lam chen po 'di dag kyang mthar thug myed par gyur te/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'di dag kyang / mthar thug pa myed par gyur cig ces de ltar smon lam shin tu bsgrubs shing phan sems
70b5(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ 'jam pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ las su rung ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ zhi ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ dul ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ nye bar zhi ba'i sems dang ldan pa/
70b6(phal chen): mnyen pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ 'khrug pa med pa'i sems dang ldan pa/ glong ba med pa'i sems dang ldan pa de ni legs par rtog pa mang zhing dad
70b7(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa yin te/ de ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sngon gyi mtha'i spyod pa mngon par bsgrubs pa'i rgyud la yid ches pa yin/
70b8(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa yang dag par bsdu ba la yid ches pa yin/ sa yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / khyad par du 'gyur ba la mngon par bsgrub pa dang / khyad par du 'gyur ba la mngon par yid
71a1(phal chen): ches pa yin/ stobs yongs su 'grub pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ myi 'jigs pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi
71a2(phal chen): chos ma 'dres pa mi 'phrogs pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi yul mtha' dang dbus myed par
71a3(phal chen): mngon par bsgrub pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul tshad myed pa'i rjes su song ba'i rjes su 'jug pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin/ 'bras bu yongs
71a4(phal chen): su grub pa la mngon par yid ches pa yin te/ mdor bsdus na byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa dang / ye shes kyi bar du shin tu bstan pa'i byin
71a5(phal chen): gyis brlabs la mngon par yid ches pa yin no/ /de yang 'di snyam du sems te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos 'di dag de ltar rgya che zhing de ltar zab la de ltar dben zhing de ltar zhi ba ste/ de ltar stong la de
71a6(phal chen): ltar mtshan ma myed cing de ltar smon pa myed pa de ltar chags pa myed pa/ de ltar gos pa myed cing de ltar tshad myed la sangs rgyas kyi chos de dag de ltar brlabs che na 'on kyang byis pa so so'i
71a7(phal chen): skye bo 'di dag lta ba ngan par ltung ba'i rgyud dang / ma rig pa'i mun nag dang / rab rib thibs pos kun nas khebs pa'i yid dang / nga rgyal gyi rgyal mtshan shin tu bsgreng pa'i yongs su rtog
71a8(phal chen): pa dang / sred pa'i dra bas mngon par ye rngam pa'i yid la bya ba dang / sgyu dang g.yo'i thibs po la rjes su spyod pa'i sems dang / bsam pa dang phrag dog dang / 'jungs pa can
71b1(phal chen): gyis kun nas 'khor ba'i lam gyi rgyud du skye ba'i kun tu 'brel pa dang / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug la spyod pa'i las shin tu bstsags pa dang / khro ba dang khon du 'dzin pas 'bar
71b2(phal chen): bar byas pa'i sems kyi me lce dang / phyin ci log dang bcas pa'i las mngon par bsgrub pa dang / 'dod pa dang sred pa'i ma rig pa dang / lta ba dang kun tu zab pa'i bag chags mtshams 'brel pa'i sems
71b3(phal chen): dang / yid dang rnam par shes pa'i sa bon gyis 'di lta ste/ khams gsum du mying dang gzugs lhan cig tu/ skyes shing tha mi dad par byung ba'i yang skye ba'i sdug bsngal gyi myu gu mngon par bskyed do/ /
71b4(phal chen): mying dang gzugs de rnam par 'phel nas skye mched drug gi tshogs 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /skye mched rnams byung ba'i phan tshun reg pa dang phrad cing 'dus pas tshor ba mngon par 'byung ngo / /tshor ba myong ba'i
71b5(phal chen): de nyid la yang dang yang mngon par dga' bas sred pa dang nye bar len pa rnam par 'phel lo/ /nye bar len pa rnam par 'phel bas/ srid pa kun tu 'byung ngo / /srid pa kun tu 'byung bas skye ba dang /
71b6(phal chen): srid pa kun tu 'byung bas skye ba dang / rga shi dang / mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal dang / yid myi bde ba dang / 'khrug pa rnams kyang 'byung bar 'gyur te/ de ltar sems
71b7(phal chen): can du ma dag gi sdug bsngal gyi phung po bdag dang bdag gi myed pa/ gsob gsog stong pa byed pa myed pa/ sems med pa rtswa dang shing dang rtsig pa dang / sgang sgong dang mig g.yor lta bu mngon par
71b8(phal chen): 'byung ba yang de ltar khong du myi chud do zhes/ de la byang chub sems dpas sems can de dag de ltar sdug bsngal gyi phung po dang 'bral mi myong ba mthong nas/ de'i phyir de'i snying rje chen po rgyas
72a1(phal chen): par 'byung ste/ sems can 'di dag ni bdag gis yongs su bskyab par bya ba dag go/ /yongs su dgrol bar bya ba dag go/ /shin tu bde ba'i sa la dgod par bya ba dag go/ /de'i phyir de'i byams pa chen po
72a2(phal chen): rgyas par 'byung / /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de ltar byang chub sems dpa' snying rje chen po dang sbyangs pa de lta bu'i rnam pa dang ldan pa'i lhag pa'i bsam pas byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po la gnas pa'i
72a3(phal chen): tshe/ dngos po thams cad la 'phangs pa'i sems yongs su spangs nas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la mos pa dang / dad pa rlabs po che'i blos sbyin pa chen po la rab tu brtson par byed de/ de 'di ltar 'di
72a4(phal chen): lta ste/ nor dang 'bru'i mdzod dang / bang ba yongs su gtang bar bya ba dag gam/ gser dang nor bu dang / mu tig dang / bai DUr+ya dang / rin po che shi la dang / byi ru dang / dngul dang / sa le sbram yongs su
72a5(phal chen): gtang bar bya ba dang / rin po che'i brgyan dang / lha lhub yongs su gtang ba 'am rta dang glang po dang / shing rta dang rkang tang dang / gzhon pa yongs su gtang ba 'am/ bran pho dang bran mo yongs su gtang ba
72a6(phal chen): 'am/ grong dang grong khyer dang / ljongs dang pho brang 'khor dang / rgyal po'i gnas yongs su gtang ba dang / bza' shing gi ra ba dang bka' thub kyi nags tshal dang gtsug lag khang yongs su gtang
72a7(phal chen): ba 'am/ chung ma dang bu dang bu mo yongs su gtang ba 'am/ sdug cing yid du 'ong ba'i dngos po thams cad yongs su gtang ba 'am/ mgo dang rkang lag dang myig dang yan lag gi dam pa dang /
72a8(phal chen): lus thams cad yongs su gtang ba 'am/ gtang bar bya ba'i dngos po de dag thams cad la chags pa myed par byas nas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la dad pa dang / mos pa'i blos
72b1(phal chen): yongs su gtong ste/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po 'di la gnas pa'i tshe gtong ba chen po rab tu byed do/ /de de ltar byams pa dang snying rje dang gtong ba'i bsam pa dang ldan pas sems can
72b2(phal chen): thams cad yongs su bskyab pa'i phyir yang dang yang 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i don yongs su tshol zhing don du gnyer to/ /de de ltar yongs su tshol zhing don du gnyer ba'i tshe
72b3(phal chen): yongs su skyo ba'i sems myi skye ste/ de'i phyir de'i yongs su myi skyo ba'i sems mngon par 'byung ngo / /yongs su skyo ba med pas gtsug lag thams cad la 'jigs pa myed pa yin/ de'i
72b4(phal chen): phyir de gtsug lag thams cad la rab tu shes pa yin te/ de de lta bu'i gtsug lag mkhas pa dang ldan pas bya ba dang myi bya ba shin tu rtogs pa'i blos sems can thams cad rab 'bring dang
72b5(phal chen): tha ma la dad pa'i tshul ji lta ba dang / ci 'os pas ci nus su snying thag pa nas yang dag pa nyid thob par bya ba'i phyir brtson par byed do/ /nan tan du byed do/ /de'i phyir de 'jig rten shes pa yin
72b6(phal chen): te/ 'jig rten shes pas dus dang tshod du ran par spyod cing ngo tsha shes pa dang / khrel yod pas bsam pa shin tu brgyan pas bdag dang gzhan gyi don du rab tu brtson par byed de/ de'i phyir de ngo
72b7(phal chen): tsha shes shing khrel yod pa yin/ sbyor ba de dag la 'ang 'byung bar spyod pa yod pa yin/ phyir myi ldog cing phyir mi ldog pa'i brtson 'grus dang stobs kyi shugs kyis rab tu thob pa yin/

73a4(phal chen): rgya chen po dang smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas brgya phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas rgya stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas bye ba brgya stong phrag mang

73b1(phal chen): su bsngo'o/ /de ltar des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag mchod pas sems can yongs su smyin par bya ba mngon par bsgrub pa yin/ de bsdu ba'i dngos po sbyin pa dang / ngag snyan pa gnyis shas che bas

73b4(phal chen): mchod pa byed cing sems can yongs su smin par bya ba la brtson pa dang / sa yongs su sbyong ba'i chos 'di dag yang dag par blangs te gnas pa de lta de ltar de'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs
73b5(phal chen): su bsngos pa de dag de bas kyang shas cher shin tu byang ba dang / yongs su dag pa dang las su rung bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste dper na/ mgar ba mkhas pas gser gyi sa le sbram/

78b2(phal chen): dga'/ /kun kyang bstan las langs gyur te/ /mkha' yi dbyings la mngon 'phags nas/ /me tog sil ma rab tu 'thor/ /legs shes bya ba'i tshig kyang brjod/ /rdo rje'i snying po 'jigs
78b3(phal chen): myed pa/ /shes rab chen po legs so legs/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa ste/ /sa 'di khyod kyis legs par bshad/ /'khor 'di rnam par dang zhing gsal/ /rnam grol zla ba 'di yang
78b4(phal chen): 'dri/ /rgyal ba'i sras kyi gong du yang / /yid gnyis rab tu brjod par mdzad/ /yid kyi rtog pa ci 'dra bas/ /sa gnyis pa ni 'thob gyur ba/ /shes rab chen pos bshad par mdzad/ /
78b5(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras rnams nyan par 'dod/ /byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sa dang po la yongs su sbyang ba byas pa de sa
78b6(phal chen): gnyis pa la mngon par mos pa yin te/ de'i sems kyi bsam pa bcu 'byung ngo / /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste drang po'i bsam pa dang / 'jam pa'i bsam pa dang las su rung ba'i
78b7(phal chen): bsam pa dang / dul ba'i bsam pa dang zhi ba'i bsam pa dang / dge ba'i bsam pa dang ma 'dres pa'i bsam pa dang / mi ldog pa'i bsam pa dang rlabs po che'i bsam pa dang / bdag
78b8(phal chen): nyid che ba'i bsam pa dang / sems kyi bsam pa bcu po 'di dag 'byung ste/ de dag gis byang chub sems dpa'i sa gnyis pa dri ma bral ba la gnas pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /
79a1(phal chen): de la byang chub sems dpa'i sa dri ma dang bral ba la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni rang bzhin gyis srog gcod pa dang bral ba yin te/ dbyig pa spangs mtshon cha spangs/ khon du 'dzin pa
79a2(phal chen): spangs shing ngo tsha dang ldan pas srog chags su gyur pa thams cad la phan pa dang bde bas phan 'dogs shing byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin te/ de yid kyi yongs su rtog pa tsam gyis kyang srog chags la
79a3(phal chen): 'tshe ba myed na sems can gzhan la sems can du 'du shes shing ched du bsams te/ lus la gtse ba chen po bya ba lta ci smos/ bdag gi longs spyod kyis yang chog shes shing gzhan gyi longs spyod la re ba
79a4(phal chen): myed pas ma byin par len pa dang bral ba yin te/ de gzhan gyis yongs su gzung ba'i dngos po yongs su bzung bar 'du shes shing rku sems nye bar bzhag ste/ chung ngu na rtswa dang lo ma yang ma byin par mi len na
79a5(phal chen): 'tsho ba'i yo byad gzhan lta ci smos/ bdag gi chung mas chog shes shing gzhan gyi chung ma la re ba med pas 'dod pas log par g.yem pa dang bral ba yin te/ de gzhan gyis yongs su gzung ba'i bud
79a6(phal chen): myed la gzhan gyi chung ma rus dang mtshan ma dang chos kyis bsrungs ba rnams la chags sems kyang myi skye na gnyis kyis gnyis phrad par bya ba lta ci smos/ yang dag par smra zhing bden par smra ba dang / dus
79a7(phal chen): su smra ba dang / tshod du smra ba la ji skad du smras pa de bzhin du byed pas/ brdzun du smra ba dang bral ba yin te/ de chung ngu na rmi lam du yang brdzun gyi tshig mi brjod na/ ched du bsams te brjod pa lta ci smos/
79a8(phal chen): de sems can gyi dbyen myi byed cing myi 'tshe ba la zhugs pas phra ma'i tshig dang bral ba yin te/ de dag dbye ba'i phyir tshu bi las thos pa pha bir snyod pa ma yin/ pha bi las thos nas tshu bir snyod pa ma yin/
79b1(phal chen): 'du ba rnams dbye bar mi byed/ bye ba rnams la dpar bas mi rnon te/ mi 'dum pa la dga' zhing mi 'dum pa la mos pa ma yin pas bden nam rdzun yang rung mi 'dum pa'i tshig mi smra'o/ /zhe gcod pa'i tshig
79b2(phal chen): dang bral ba yin te/ snyogs pa dang / blang ba dang / rtsub pa dang / gzhan la gnod pa dang / zhe sdang bar gyur pa dang / nyes pa ngor brjod pa dang / nyes pa ngor brjod pa la gzhol ba dang / grong gi
79b3(phal chen): tshig dang / ma rabs kyi tshig dang / gzungs su bzung ba ma yin pa dang / rnar mi snyan pa dang / khro ba dang gshe ba las byung ba dang / snying na bar byed pa dang / yid yongs su gdung bar byed
79b4(phal chen): pa dang / myi snyan pa dang / yid du mi 'ong ba dang / bdag dang gzhan gyi sems ma rung bar byed pa'i tshig gi rnam pa de lta bu spangs te/ gang 'di 'jam pa dang yid du 'ong ba dang / snyan pa dang /
79b5(phal chen): gzungs su bzung ba dang / rnar bong ba dang / snying du sdug pa dang / pho brang 'khor gyi tshig dang / rtsig pa dang / gsal ba dang / 'go ba dang mnyan par 'os pa dang / mi gnas pa dang / skye bo
79b6(phal chen): mang po dga' bar 'gyur ba dang / skye bo mang po'i yid du 'ong ba dang / mkhas pas bsngags pa dang / sems can thams cad la phan zhing bde bar 'gyur ba dang / yid bde bar byed pa dang yid
79b7(phal chen): sems par byed pa dang / bdag dang gzhan gyi sems dang bar byed pa dang / 'dod chags dang zhe sdang dang gti mug dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad zhi bar byed pa'i tshig gi rnam pa de lta bu
79b8(phal chen): dag brjod do/ /tshig kyal pa spangs pa yin te/ legs par lan glon pa'i tshig dang / dus su smra ba dang / bden par smra ba dang / don du smra ba dang / chos su smra ba dang / rigs
80a1(phal chen): par smra ba dang / 'dul bar smra ba dang / dus la bab par shin tu go ba'i gtan tshig dang bcas par smra bar de chung ngu na gzhad gad du bya ba tsam gyi tshig la yang yongs su spang bar bya ba
80a2(phal chen): yongs su spong na dgos pa don du gnyer cing tshig gis rnam par 'khrug pa lta ci smos/ chags sems mi bskyed pa yin/ de gzhan gyi nor dang / gzhan gyi 'dod pa dang / gzhan gyi dbang
80a3(phal chen): ba'i yo byad gzhan gyis yongs su gzung ba la ji ltar na/ gang gzhan gyi yin pa de dag bdag gir 'byung zhes ste/ chags sems mi bskyed mi re mi smod cing 'dod pa'i sems mi bskyed do/ /
80a4(phal chen): gnod sems dang bral ba yin te/ sems can thams cad la byams pa'i sems dang phan pa'i sems dang snying brtse ba'i sems dang / bde ba'i sems dang / 'jam pa'i sems dang /
80a5(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad la phan gdags pa'i sems dang / 'byung po thams cad la snying brtse ba'i sems dang ldan pa dang / gang 'di khro ba dang / mdung bar 'dzin pa dang / thab dang dri ma dang gnod
80a6(phal chen): sems dang khong khro ba la stsogs pa de dag spangs te/ gang 'di phan pa dang ldan pa/ byams pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la phan pa dang bde bar bya ba'i phyir rnam par rtog cing / rnam
80a7(phal chen): par dpyod pa de dag la rnam par rtog pa yin/ yang dag par lta ba dang ldan zhing ngo mtshar dang bkra shis dang / ngang tshul ngan pa'i lta ba sna tshogs dang bral ba yin te/ lta ba drang zhing g.yo med
80a8(phal chen): la sgyu med pas sangs rgyas dang / chos dang dge 'dun la bsam pa yin te/ de dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par bsrung zhing 'di ltar sems kyi bsam pa mngon
80b1(phal chen): par bsgrub ste/ sems can rnams kyi ngan song dang ngan 'gro dang / log par ltung ba yod pa gang yang rung ste/ de dag thams cad mi dge ba bcu'i lam 'di dag yongs su blangs pa'i rgyu las byung gis bdag
80b2(phal chen): gis ni 'di ltar bdag nyid yang dag pa'i nan tan la gnas te gzhan yang dag pa'i nan tan la dgod par bya'o/ /yang dag pa'i nan tan la gnas shing gzhan yang dag pa'i nan tan la dgod par bya'o/ /'di ni
80b3(phal chen): gnas med skabs med pa ste/ 'di ni mi srid do zhes nas yang de 'di ltar rnam par dpyod de/ mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag yongs su gzung ba'i rgyus sems can dmyal ba dang byol song gi skye gnas dang /
80b4(phal chen): gshin rje'i 'jig rten gyi lam gyi rgyud du skye ba rnams yod par gyur to/ /dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bzung bas ni mir skye ba las stsogs pa srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du skye ba yod par gyur to/ /de'i gong du dge ba bcu'i
80b5(phal chen): las kyi lam 'di dag nyi tse'i sems dang khams gsum pas skrag pa'i yid dang / snying rje chen po med pa dang / gzhan la thos pa'i sgra'i rjes su 'brang ba'i shes rab kyis rnam par yongs su bsgoms
80b6(phal chen): na nyan thos kyi theg pa yongs su bsgrub po/ /de'i gong du gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa dang / rang mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang / snying rje chen po dang / thabs mkhas pa med pa dang / rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zab par khong du chud pas yongs su sbyangs na rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa yongs su sgrub bo/ /de'i gong du yangs shing tshad med pa'i sems dang / snying rje zhing snying rje dang ldan pa dang / thabs mkhas pas yang dag par gzung ba dang / smon
80b7(phal chen): lam chen po shin tu btab pa dang / sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes rgya chen po la dmyigs pas yongs su sbyangs na byang chub sems dpa'i
80b8(phal chen): sa yongs su dag pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par dag pa'i spyod pa rgya chen po yongs su bsgrub par 'gyur ro/ /de'i gong du dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag nyid rnam pa'i mchog
81a1(phal chen): thams cad dang ldan par yongs su sbyangs pas stobs bcu'i stobs thob par 'gyur ba dang / mi 'jigs pa bzhi thob pa nas rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas
81a2(phal chen): kyi chos yongs su 'grub pa yongs su bsgrub po/ /de lta bas na bdag gis dge ba bcu'i las mngon par bsgrub du 'dra ba la rnam pa thams cad du yongs su sbyang zhing mngon par bsgrub pa la brtson par bya'o

82a1(phal chen): de ltar na mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag ni sdug bsngal gyi phung po che zhing tshad med pa sdud par 'gyur gyis mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag bdag gis spangs te chos la
82a2(phal chen): dga' zhing mos par dga' bar gnas par bya'o zhes te/ de mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam 'di dag spangs nas dge ba bcu'i lam la gnas shing gzhan yang de nyid la rab tu bzhog go/ /sems can

82a5(phal chen): ste/ blo gros mi mnyam zhing bsam pa mi mnyam pa/ log pa'i lam thib por rgyu ba yin gyis de dag bdag gi bden pa'i lam dang / yang dag par lta ba'i lam/ de bzhin nyid ji lta ba bzhin

82b3(phal chen): rib kyi ling thog gis bsgribs shing mun pa thibs po'i nang du song bas shes rab kyi snang ba dang ring du gyur te/ 'khor ba'i mya ngan chen po la gnas shing lta ba ngan pa'i mya ngan la gzhol bar 'gyur ba

82b7(phal chen): rab tu zhugs pa/ long bar gyur pa dge ba'i mgon med pa/ 'byung ba ma yin pa la 'byung bar lta ba/ bdud kyi zhags pas bcings pa/ yul gyi rkun pos zin pa/ bdud kyi bsam
82b8(phal chen): pa thibs por nub pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bsam pa dang ring du gyur pa yin gyis de dag bdag gis rnam pa de lta bu'i 'khor ba'i dgon pa dang / mya ngan brgal dka' ba las bsgral te/
83a1(phal chen): 'jigs pa med pa'i gnas thams cad mkhyen pa'i grong rdal chen po gtse ba myed par rab tu dgod par bya'o/ /kye ma sems can 'di dag ni chu bo chen po'i gling du bying zhing 'dod pa'i

83a3(phal chen): mthus shin tu bcom pa/ brtag pa'i 'dzin mthu med par 'dod pa/ gnod sems dang 'tshe ba dang / rnam pa mang po'i rjes su spyod pa 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i chu srin pos khrid pa 'dod pa'i yon
83a4(phal chen): tan thibs po'i gling du zhugs pa/ smon pa'i 'dod chags kyi 'dam du thogs pa/ de'i nga rgyal gyi dbye ba chen por ma byams pa/ rten mang por skye mched kyi grong rdal nas ma 'phags par dge ba'i
83a5(phal chen): bskal pa myed pa yin gyis/ de dag bdag gis snying rje chen po dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs kyi shugs kyis bton te/ thams cad mkhyen pa rin po che'i gling 'tshe ba med pa rdul myed pa zhi ba

83b1(phal chen): bdag dang bdag la mngon par zhen zhing phung po'i gnas las ma 'phags pa phyin ci log bzhi la rab tu zhugs pa/ skyed mched drug gi grong la shin tu gnas pa/ 'byung ba chen po bzhi'i sprul gyis

83b4(phal chen): ' byung ba yod kyang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi blo can yin gyis de dag bdag gis sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya chen po'i blo gros dang bsam pa yangs pa'i theg pa chen po bla na med pa thams cad
83b5(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su bstan pas rab tu dgod par bya'o snyam mo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de ltar tshul khrims kyi stobs dang mthu de lta bu dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
83b6(phal chen): snying rje dang byams pa mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pa/ sems can thams cad kyis ma gcos pa'i bshes gnyen du gyur pa/ sems can thams cad yongs su ma btang ba bya ba dang
83b7(phal chen): mi bya ba mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa dri ma med pa la gnas pa de'i lta ba rgya chen po dang / smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas mang po rab tu snang bar
83b8(phal chen): gyur te/ lta ba rgya chen po dang smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas brgya phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas brgya stong phrag mang po dang /
84a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bye ba brgya stong mang po dang / sangs rgyas khrag khrig mang po dang / sangs rgyas khrag khrig brgya phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas khrag khrig stong phrag mang po dang /

107a3(phal chen): bzla ba'i phyir rab tu rtsom ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa shin tu rgyal bar dga' ba 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni/ de bas kyang nyams par mi 'gyur ba'i chos nyid kyis dran pa dang ldan
107a4(phal chen): pa yin/ shin tu nges par rtogs pa'i ye shes kyis blo gros dang ldan pa yin/ mdo'i don dang tshul dang ldem po ngag khong du chud pas rigs dang ldan pa yin/ bdag dang gzhan gyi rjes su bsrungs bas
107a5(phal chen): ngo tsha shes shing khrel yod pa yin/ sdom pa dang tshul ma bor bas dga' ba dang ldan pa yin/ gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas shing shin tu brtags pas blo dang ldan pa yin/ gzhan gyi dring mi
107a6(phal chen): 'jog pas ye shes dang ldan pa yin/ don dang don ma yin pa'i tshig yang dag par dbye ba la mkhas pas shes rab dang ldan pa yin/ bsgom pa mngon par bsgrub pa la mkhas pas mngon par shes
107a7(phal chen): pa bsgrub pa thob pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi rjes su 'brel bas thabs la mkhas pa yin/ bsod nams kyi tshogs nye bar stsogs pas ngoms mi shes pa yin/ ye shes kyi tshogs yongs
107a8(phal chen): su tshol bas brtson 'grus rgyun mi 'chad pa yin/ byams pa dang snying rje chen po'i tshogs yang dag stsogs pas skyo ba med pa'i bsam pa dang ldan pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
107b1(phal chen): stobs dang mi 'jigs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa yongs su tshol bas snyom las med par yongs su tshol ba la brtson pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsgrub pa dang / rgyan
107b2(phal chen): mngon par shom pas mngon par bsgrub pa'i yid dang ldan pa yin/ mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po yang dag par bsgrub pas dge ba rnam pa sna tshogs la brtson pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi
107b3(phal chen): rgyan yongs su tshol bas/ rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par brtson pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' dang chos smra ba thams cad la rim gro byas pas bsnyen bkur dang sri zhu chen po'i ngang tshul can yin/ byang chub kyi
107b4(phal chen): sems dang thabs mkhas pa chen po'i tshul dang ldan par 'jig rten du rgyu bas khong khro ba med pa'i sems dang ldan pa yin/ sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya ba la mngon par brtson pas nyin mtshan du
107b5(phal chen): gzhan du sems pa'i yid yongs su spangs pa yin te/ de de ltar mngon par brtson pas sbyin pas kyang sems can yongs su smin par byed do/ /ngag snyan pa dang don bsgrub pa dang / don 'thun pa dang gzugs
107b6(phal chen): kyi lus kun tu bstan pa dang / chos bshad pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa brjod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i che ba nyid smos pa dang / 'khor ba'i nyes pa bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi
107b7(phal chen): yon tan yongs su grag par bya ba dang / rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul pa chen po mngon par bsgrub pa dang / bya ba dang thabs rnam pa sna tshogs kyis sbyor bas sems can yongs su smin par byed do/ /de ltar sems
107b8(phal chen): can yongs su smin par bya ba la mngon par brtson pa dang ldan zhing sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi rjes su song ba'i bsam pa can dge ba'i rtsa ba phyir mi ldog pa'i sbyor ba dang ldan pa/ khyad par can gyi chos yongs su
108a1(phal chen): btsal ba la mngon par brtson pa de gang 'di 'jig rten na yod pa'i yi ge dang gtsug lag dang / lag brda dang / grangs dang / rtsi dang rtsis dang / shod thabs las stsogs pa dang / khams kyi cho ga dang /

108a8(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i lta ba rgya chen po dang / smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas mang po snang bar 'gyur te/ lta ba rgya chen po dang smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas brgya phrag mang po dang / sangs
108b1(phal chen): rgyas stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas brgya stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas bye ba brgya stong phrag mang po dang / sangs rgyas khrag khrig mang po dang / sangs rgyas khrag khrig brgya phrag mang po dang /

108b3(phal chen): nas bsam pa rgya chen pos rim gro byed do/ /bkur bstir byed do/ /sti stang byed do/ /mchod pa byed do/ /na bza' dang bsod snyoms dang / gzims cha dang / snyun gyi rkyen sman dang / yo byad dag kyang dbul zhing byang
108b4(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i bde ba'i yo byad thams cad kyang yongs su 'bul lo/ /dge 'dun gyi tshogs rnams la yang dag par mchod pa byed de/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
108b5(phal chen): tu yongs su bsngo'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag la rim gro byed cing de dag las rim gro dang zhe sa dang sti stang du chos bstan pa nyan to len to/ 'dzin to/ /
108b6(phal chen): thos nas kyang ci tshul bzhin du nan tan gyis yang dag par bsgrubs te/ de dag las phal cher de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi bstan pa la rab tu 'byung ngo / /rab tu byung nas kyang thos pa 'dzin pa'i gzungs
108b7(phal chen): rab tu thob pa'i chos smra bar 'gyur ba yin/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa shin tu rgyal bar dka' ba 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de'i dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag bskal pa du mar shin tu byang ba dang /
108b8(phal chen): yongs su dag pa dang / 'od rab tu gsal bar gnas so/ /bskal pa brgya phrag du ma dang / bskal pa stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa brgya stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa bye ba brgya stong phrag du
109a1(phal chen): ma dang / bskal pa khrag khrig du ma dang / bskal pa khrag khrig brgya phrag du ma dang / bskal pa khrag khrig stong phrag du ma dang / bskal pa khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dang / bskal pa bye ba khrag

109a3(phal chen): btab na de bas kyang yongs su 'tsher ro/ /yongs su dag par 'gyur ro/ /'od shin tu gastsal zhing dang bar 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa shin tu rgyal bar
109a4(phal chen): dka' ba 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thabs dang shes rab kyis rnam par spyad pa yang de bas kyang shin tu byang ba dang / yongs su dag pa dang rab tu 'od gsal zhing dang ba yin/ ye
109a5(phal chen): shes kyi sbyor ba'i yon tan mngon par bsgrub pa dang ldan pa yin/ mi 'phrogs shing shin tu brtags pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di lta ste dper na/ nyi ma dang zla ba dang / skar ma dang rgyu skar gyi
109a6(phal chen): gzhal med khang gi 'od snang ba ni rlung gi dkyil 'khor mi 'phrogs shing rlung dang thun mong du mi spyod pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa shin tu rgyal bar dka' ba 'di la gnas
109a7(phal chen): pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thabs dang shes rab dang ye shes dang sems kyis shin tu brtags pa dang ldan pa yang nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyis mi 'phrogs pa yin/ 'jig rten pa dang thun mong du mi spyod pa yin/
109a8(phal chen): de'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu las bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa shas che ba yin te/ lhag ma rnams kyang ci tshul ci nus su mi bsgrub pa ma yin no/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang
109b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i shin tu rgyal bar dka' ba zhes bya ba byang chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa mdor bstan pa'o/ /de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni phal cher lha'i rgyal por dga' ldan du 'gyur te/ sems
109b2(phal chen): can thams cad kyi mu stegs kyi gnas thams cad rnam par zlog pa la mkhas shing mthu yod pa yin/ de sbyin pa 'am ngag snyan pa 'am/ don bsgrub pa 'am/ don 'thun pas dge ba'i rtsa ba gang ci rtsom yang rung
109b3(phal chen): ste/ de thams cad ji ltar na sems can thams cad kyi mchog tu 'gyur/ gtso bor 'gyur/ thu bor 'gyur/ phul du 'gyur/ dam par 'gyur/ bla na med par 'gyur/ 'dren par 'gyur/ yongs su 'dren
109b4(phal chen): par 'gyur ba nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la brten pa'i bar du 'gyur snyam ste/ sangs rgyas yid la bya ba dang / chos yid la bya ba dang / dge 'dun yid la bya ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' yid la

109b6(phal chen): rnam pa'i mchog thams cad dang ldan pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi bar du yid la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba yin te/ de 'dod na skad cig yud tsam thang cig tu ting nge 'dzin khrag khrig phrag stong rab tu 'thob cing
