112a1(phal chen): se mo do yang 'bul/ /lha'i dbang po dbang bsgyur lha tshogs mang po dang / /steng gi mkha' la 'khod cing rin chen sprin yangs pa/ /rgyal ba mchod pa'i don tu bde bar gshegs la 'thor/ /dga' ba'i

112a3(phal chen): byung / /rgyal ba'i gsung ni yid 'ong nyon mongs gdung ba sel/ /chos rnams thams cad stong zhing mtshan ma med/ /nam mkha'i dbyings dang mtshungs mnyam rnam dag rnams mi rtog /'gro dang gnas las rnam
112a4(phal chen): 'das ma lus spros pa med/ /de bzhin nyid du chos rnams yang dag mnyam mi rtog /chos rnams kun la snang ba khong du su chud pa/ /de la dngos dang dngos med g.yo ba gang yang med/ /snying rje brtse bas 'gro ba
112a5(phal chen): dgrol phyir brtson pa ni/ /de dang de dag rgyal sras chos kyi skus skyed pa'i/ /mtshan ma thams cad spangs shing sbyin pa'i spyad pa spyod/ /tshul khrims shin tu sems dam sngon nas zhi zhing dul/ /'gro ba'i don tu chos
112a6(phal chen): kyi ye shes ma nyams bzod/ /brtson 'grus stobs dang ldan zhing chos rnams kun kyis dben/ /nyon mongs bstsal zhing rnam dag bsam gtan tshul la zhugs/ /dngos po thams cad snga nas zhi zhing
112a7(phal chen): rnam par phye/ /ye shes spyod dang stobs phyug rtag tu 'gro don brtson/ /rgyal sras de dag sdig zhi che ba nyid dang ldan/ /de skad sgra dbyangs snyan pa stong grangs brjod byas nas/ /lha'i bu mo mi smra dad par thub la
112a8(phal chen): lta/ /rdo rje'i snying po 'jigs med la/ /thar pa'i zla la yang smras pa/ /sa mchog lnga yi gong ma de/ /rnam pa ci 'dras 'grub par 'gyur/ /byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/
112b1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i sa lnga pa las lam yongs su rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa drug pa la 'jug go/ /de chos mnyam pa nyid bcus
112b2(phal chen): 'jug ste/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad mtshan ma med pa mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad mtshan nyid med pa mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad mi skye ba mnyam pa nyid dang /
112b3(phal chen): chos thams cad ma byung ba mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad dben pa la mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad snga nas rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad spros pa med pa mnyam
112b4(phal chen): pa nyid dang / chos thams cad blang ba med pa dang dor ba med pa mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad sgyu ma dang rmi lam dang mig yor dang sgra brnyan dang / chu'i zla ba dang / gzugs brnyan dang / sprul pa dang
112b5(phal chen): mtshungs pa mnyam pa nyid dang / chos thams cad dngos po yod pa dang / dngos po med pa dang / gnyis ka ma yin pa mnyam pa nyid dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /chos mnyam pa nyid bcu po 'di
112b6(phal chen): dag gis byang chub sems dpa' sa drug pa la 'jug go/ /de chos thams cad la rang bzhin de 'dra ba rab tu rtog cing dpyod pa dang / 'thun par sems shing mi 'thun par mi byed pas byang chub

123b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dus gsum thugs su chud pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sems can gyi mos pa'i khyad par tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan dang /
123b5(phal chen): gzugs dang sku sna tshogs ston pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang dbang po tha dad pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung brjod pas/
123b6(phal chen): sems can yongs su smin par mdzad pa la 'jug go/ /sems can rnams kyi sems dang spyod pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ye shes 'byam klas pa
123b7(phal chen): thugs su chud pa tshad myed pa la 'jug go/ /nyan thos kyi theg pas byung ba la mos pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi lam shin tu bstan pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa tshad
123b8(phal chen): med pa la 'jug cing mos par byed do/ /rang sangs rgyas kyi ye shes yang dag par bsgrub pa shin tu rdzogs par bya ba tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes zab
124a1(phal chen): mo'i sgor 'jug pa bstan pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i spyod pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan
124a2(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi theg pa chen po yang dag par bsgrub pa la 'jug pa shin tu bstan pa tshad med pa la 'jug go/ /de 'di snyam du sems te de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
124a3(phal chen): pa'i rnams kyi spyod yul ni de ltar tshad med pa ste/ de ni bskal pa brgya phrag khrag khrig dang / bskal pa stong phrag khrag khrig dang / bskal pa brgya stong phrag khrag khrig nas de snyed kyi
124a4(phal chen): bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gis kyang grangs par ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyod yul de bdag gis lhun gyis grub par bya'o/ /rtog pa med pa dang rnam par rtog pa
124a5(phal chen): med par yongs su rdzogs par bya'o zhes de de ltar shin tu brtags pa'i ye shes dang mngon par shes pa dang ldan zhing rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par mngon par brtson pa ni/ thabs dang shes rab kyis yongs
124a6(phal chen): su bsgoms pa'i lam gyi tshogs rgya chen po'i ye shes la mi g.yo ba'i tshul gyis yongs su gnas pa yin/ de skad cig gcig tu yang lam mngon par bsgrub pa las ldang bar mi byed de/ de 'gro
124a7(phal chen): yang de lta bu'i ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa yin/ 'greng ba dang 'dug pa dang nyal ba dang rmi lam dag tu sgrib pa med cing spyod lam thams cad la gnas kyang rnam pa 'di lta bu'i 'du shes yid
124a8(phal chen): la bya ba dang mi 'bral ba yin/ de'i sems bskyed pa re re la yang byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu dang byang chub sems dpa'i sa bcu la yang dag par bsgrub pa yang dag par 'byung
124b1(phal chen): ngo / de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de snying rje chen po sngon du btang ba'i sems bskyed pa byung ba re re zhing yang sangs rgyas kyi chos yang dag par bsgrub
124b2(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi don du yongs su bsngo bas de la gang sangs rgyas kyi ye shes yongs su tshol zhing sems can rnams la dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su gtong ba 'di ni de'i
124b3(phal chen): sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang nyon mongs pa'i yongs su gdung ba thams cad rab tu zhi ba 'di ni de'i tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang snying rje dang byams pa sngon du 'gro bas sems
124b4(phal chen): can thams cad la 'tshig pa med pa 'di ni de'i bzod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang gong nas gong du dge ba'i chos tshol bas ma ngoms par dam bca' ba 'di ni brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /
124b5(phal chen): gang thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mngon du bya ba'i phyir 'gyod pa med pa'i lam dang ldan pa 'di ni de'i bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang rang bzhin gyis ma skyes pa mngon du gyur pa 'di ni de'i
124b6(phal chen): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang ye shes tshad med pa mngon par bsgrub pa 'di ni de'i thabs mkhas pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang gong nas gong du ye shes la dmigs shing mngon par
124b7(phal chen): bsgrub pa 'di ni de'i smon lam gyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang phas kyi rgol ba thams cad dang bdud kyi tshogs thams cad kyis lam yongasu mi mchod pa 'di ni de'i stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /gang
124b8(phal chen): chos thams cad la yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du rtog pa 'di ni de'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i sa ring du song ba 'di la gnas
125a1(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu po de dag de ltar yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi yang yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro/ /byin gyis rlabs
125a2(phal chen): bcu dang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos sum bcu rtsa bdun dang / rnam par thar pa'i sgo gsum dang / mdor bsdu na byang chub kyi yan lag gi chos thams cad skad cig skad gcig tu yongs su rdzogs par

125a5(phal chen): 'on te ma yin gyis sa bcu po thams cad la'ang de bzhin du yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sa bcu po kun la'ang byang chub

125a7(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i sa 'di ni nan tan du bya ba'i spyod pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa ye shes dang mngon par shes pa'i spyod pa yongs su gnon
125a8(phal chen): pa ste/ de ltar kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po la ni smon lam thams cad la lhag par dmigs pas byang chub sems dpa'i byang chub kyi yan lag thams cad yongs su rdzogs par
125b1(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /gnyis pa la sems kyi dri ma thams cad bstsal bas gsum pa la smon lam rnam par 'phel ba dang / chos kyi snang ba thob pas/ bzhi pa la lam la 'jug pas/ lnga pa
125b2(phal chen): la 'jig rten gyi spyod pa'i rjes su 'brang bas/ drug pa la chos zab mo'i sgor 'jug pas byang chub kyi yan lag thams cad yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa 'di

125b4(phal chen): nas bzung ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa'i bar du byang chub sems dpas mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa'i sbyor ba'i yan lag de dag byang chub sems dpa'i sa brgyad
125b5(phal chen): par yan lag lhun gyi grub par yongs su 'grub bo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ kun nas nyon mongs shing rnam par dag pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang shin tu dag pa'i 'jig rten gyi
125b6(phal chen): khams dag gis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi bar ni smon lam dang thabs dang shes rab dang mngon par shes pa'i stobs dang shugs chen po ma gtogs par mdo 'dod brgal bar mi nus so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras
125b7(phal chen): de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa 'dres pa dang yongs su dag pa'i bar yang smon pa dang / thabs dang shes rab dang / mngon par shes pa dang / ye shes kyi stobs dang shugs chen po ma gtogs
125b8(phal chen): mod 'dod rgyal bar mi nus so/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnam par grol ba'i zla bas smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'o na ci byang chub sems dpa' sa bdun rnams la byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nyon
126a1(phal chen): mongs par yid ches par bya ba yin nam/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po rab tu dga' ba nyid bzung ba yan
126a2(phal chen): cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad byang chub tu yongs su bsngos pa'i dbang gis nyon mongs pa'i rnyog pa dang bral bar byar 'os pa'i tshul gyi lam mnyam pa nyid kyis yid ches pas bya ste/ de
126a3(phal chen): tsam gyis sa bdun po rnams nyon mongs pa'i spyod pa las yang dag par 'das shes ni mi bya'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni lha rdzas kyi glang
126a4(phal chen): po rin po che la zhon zhing gling bzhi dag tu'ang 'gro/ mi'i sdug bsngal dang phongs pa dang kun nas nyon mongs pa'i nyes pa rnams kyang rab tu shes te 'on kyang nyes pa de dag gis gos par mi 'gyur ro/ /
126a5(phal chen): de tsam gyis mi'i lus las yongs su 'das pa'ang ma yin te/ nam mi'i lus spangs ste tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du skyes par gyur pa de'i tshe ni tshangs pa'i gzhal med khang na gnas shing stong gis
126a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams kyang mthong / de dag du 'ang 'gro tshangs pa'i gzugs brnyan yang kun tu ston te mi zhes kyang mi brjod do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i sa dang po bzung

126a8(phal chen): pas kun nas nyon mongs pa de dag gis gos par yang mi 'gyur ro/ /'on kyang de tsam gyi sa bdun po rnams la nyon mongs pa'i nyes pa rnams las yang dag par 'das shes ni mi bya ste/ nam sbyor
126b1(phal chen): ba can gyi spyod pa thams cad spangs te sa bdun po nas sa brgyad pa yongs su non par gyur te/ byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa yongs su dag pa la zhon zhing 'gro ba thams cad du rgyu ba'i tshe kun nas nyon

126b3(phal chen): dpa'i sa bdun pa 'di la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni 'dod chags las stsogs pa'i nyon mongs pa mang po thams cad las kyang shin tu shas che bar 'da' ste/ byang chub sems
126b4(phal chen): dpa'i sa bdun pa 'di la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpa' de ni nyon mongs pa can zhes mi bya/ nyon mongs pa med pa zhes kyang mi bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nyon mongs pa thams cad rgyu ba med pas

126b8(phal chen): du yang dag par 'das pa yin/ gang 'di dag dge ba'i lam yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bsngags pa de dag gi rjes su rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par 'brang ba yin/ gang yang byang chub

127a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' ma gtogs par su'ang de dang bsam pa 'am sbyor ba mnyam pa med do/ /'di ltar yang dag 'di dag bsam gtan rnams dang / ting nge 'dzin dag dang snyoms par 'jug pa rnams dang / mngon

127a8(phal chen): shes bya ba dang / rab tu phye ba'i don gyi mdzod ces bya ba dang / chos ji lta ba bzhin du rnam pa byed pa zhes bya ba dang / rtsa ba shin tu gnas pas brtan pa zhes bya ba dang / ye shes dang mngon

127b3(phal chen): 'jug go/ /de thabs dang shes rab kyis yongs su sbyangs pa'i ting nge 'dzin de dag rab tu thob pa dang / snying rje dang snying brtse ba'i mthus nyan thos kyi sa las 'das pa yin/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sa las
127b4(phal chen): 'das pa yin/ shes rab dang ye shes kyis rnam par dpyod pa'i sa mngon sum du gyur pa yin/ de ltar de byang chub sems dpa'i sa bdun pa 'di la gnas pa'i tshe/ lus kyi las tshad med pa mtshan
127b5(phal chen): ma dang bral ba rab tu 'byung ngo / /ngag gi las tshad med pa mtshan ma dang bral ba rab tu 'byung ngo / /yid kyi las mtshan ma dang bral ba shin tu rnam par sbyangs pa mi skye ba'i chos kyi bzod pas

128a1(phal chen): po 'di la ni rang gi blo'i spyod yul rnam par spyod pa rab tu thob pas nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi mi 'phrogs pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste dper na/ rgyal

128a7(phal chen): pa yin te/ khyad par gong du btsal ba'i brtson 'grus kyang yongs su mi gtong ngo / /yongs su btsal ba'i brtson 'grus des kyang yang dag pa'i mthar gnas te/ khyad par gong ma shin tu thob

128b5(phal chen): ba'i thabs la mkhas shing rlung la mkhas pa dang / chu la mkhas pa ni rgya mtsho chen po'i chu'i nyes pas mi gos so/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/

128b7(phal chen): de ltar de ye shes kyi stobs dang shugs thob pa ni ting nge 'dzin dang ye shes kyi stobs dang shugs kyis mngon par bsgrubs pa'i blo dang thabs dang shes rab kyi stobs dang shugs chen pos 'khor ba'i
128b8(phal chen): sgo yang ston la mya ngan las 'das pa'i bsam pa dang yang mi bral ba yin/ 'khor mang pos kun nas bskor bar snang yang rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par sems kyi dben pa yang rab tu thob pa yin/
129a1(phal chen): khams gsum du skye ba yang smon lam gyi dbang po mngon par bsgrub la 'jig rten gyi nyes pas kyang mi gos pa yin/ zhi zhing rab tu zhi ba'ang yin la thabs kyis kyang rab tu 'bar te/ de ltar
129a2(phal chen): 'bar yang tshig par mi 'gyur ba yin/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la'ang yongs su 'jug la nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi sa las kyang phyir mi ldog pa yin/ sangs rgyas gyi yul gyi mthil du yang phyin
129a3(phal chen): la bdud kyi yul na'ang 'dug par snang ba yin/ bdud kyi lam bzhi las kyang yang dag par 'das la bdud kyi yul dang spyod yul yang yang dag par ston pa yin/ mu stegs can gyi gnas thams cad na'ang 'dug par

140b8(phal chen): yang dag par rgyu zhing 'byung ba yin/ ngag gi las kha na ma tho ba shin tu med pa yang dag par rgyu zhing 'byung ba yin/ yid kyi las kha na ma tho ba shin tu med cing ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ye shes rjes
141a1(phal chen): su 'brang ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas dbang bsgyur ba snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba thabs mkhas pas shin tu rnam par phye ba smon lam gyis shin tu mngon par

152b1(phal chen): yang dag par shes pas sa bcu rnam par dgod cing / shin tu bstan pa rnam par phye ba la yang dag par 'jug go/ /nges pa'i tshig tha dad pa yang dag par shes pas sa'i lam ji lta ba

153a4(phal chen): gnas pa chos smra ba chen po'i go 'phang la gnas pa'i tshe/ don dang ldan pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yin/ chos dang ldan pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yin/ ye shes mngon par
153a5(phal chen): bsgrub pa dang ldan pa'i bzungs rab tu thob pa yin/ snang ba dang ldan pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yin/ blo gros bzang po dang ldan pa'i gzungs dang / dbyibs dang ldan pa'i gzungs

153a7(phal chen): tshogs kyi mdzod dang ldan pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yin/ de gzungs de dag la stsogs pa gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs myed pa phrag bcu yongs su tshangs par thob par 'gyur ro/ /
153a8(phal chen): gzungs kyi sgo brgya stong grangs myed pa phrag bcu dang ldan pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag la mkhas pas de snyed du tshad med pa nyid dang ldan pa'i spobs pa rnam par phye ba'i sgos chos ston to/ /

153b6(phal chen): 'dug na/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ chos kyi stan la 'dug cing sems can rnams la bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par phye

153b8(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa yin/ de 'dod na chos kyi stan la 'dug cing dbyangs gcig gis 'khor thams cad du sgra skad sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pas yang dag par go bar byed do/ /'dod na sgra

154b8(phal chen): gshegs pa de dag re res kyang de snyed kyi sems can tshad myed pa la chos rnam pa tha dad par shin tu bstan te/ sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud re re la de snyed du chos nye bar bsgrub pa tshad myed pa

181a8(phal chen): bstsags byas nas/ /snying rje brtse ldan sa yi gong ma yongs su gnon/ /'gro phyir byams sems tshul khrims thos dang yon tan ldan/ /dri med dri bral rang bzhin yang dag bsam pa yi
181b1(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad me gsum 'bar bar mthong gyur nas/ /gsum pa rnam yangs blo yis 'gro ba'i don du gnon/ /sdug bsngal mi rtag nad pa zug rngus mi bde ba'i/ /khams
181b2(phal chen): gsum rtag tu sdug bsngal brgya yi me 'bar ba'i/ /'dus byas nyes mthong rgyal ba'i legs pa mngon mos shing / /ye shes 'od 'phro yangs ldan 'od 'phro yod pa gnon/ /dran dang blo ldan
181b3(phal chen): lam gyi ye shes thob gyur cing / /sa mchog de la sangs rgyas brgya stong bsnyen bkur nas/ /mi yis gartso bo'i yon tan rtag tu dran byed cing / /'gro ba kun gyis thub dka' rgyal bar
181b4(phal chen): dka' ba gnon/ /ye shes blo gros thabs dang shes rab blo dpyod pas/ /'gro don mtha' yas sna tshogs bya ba bstan byas shing / /stobs bcu mchod pa sems can don rnams bsgrub byas te/ /
181b5(phal chen): mi skye mngon sum mtha' yas sa drug yongs su gnon/ /'jig rten kun tu 'gro bas shes dka' spyod byed cing / /bdag bral byed med yod dang med pa rnam sel ba'i/ /rang bzhin stong chos
181b6(phal chen): yan lag bcu gnyis rab 'byung zhes/ /phra zhing rno ba'i sems ldan bdun pa yongs su gnon/ /thabs dang shes rab sems yangs rab tu thob gyur cing / /ring du song ba gdul dka' ring du song ba gnon/ /
181b7(phal chen): rang bzhin dul zhing zhi phyir du ma'i sems spangs te/ /de nas nam mkha' 'dra ba yi mi g.yo yongasu gnon/ /de la mkhas pa'i ye shes las rnams sna tshogs phyir/ /zhi ba de las bslang zhing myi yi mchog tu
181b8(phal chen): bsnabs/ /dbang bcu ldan zhing 'jig rten yang dag nyid dpyod pa'i/ /rang bzhin chen po 'gro phyir legs pa'i blo gros gnon/ /'di la shin tu phra bar 'jig rten kun dpyad cing / /sems can
182a1(phal chen): thibs po'i spyod ldan nyon mongs las dpyad de/ /de dag gdul bas spyod pa'i yon tan mang po gnon/ /bde gshegs mdzod thob don gyi dam pa rab tu ston/ /dkar chos rim gyis
182a2(phal chen): de 'dra'i spyod dang ldan gyur pas/ /sa dgu'i bar du bsod nams ye shes tshogs thob cing / /rgyal ba rnams kyi stobs mchog don dam mngon 'dod pa/ /ye shes yon tan dbang bskur sangs rgyas
182a3(phal chen): kun nas thob/ /brgya stong phrag bcu'i ting 'dzin grangs med gang yod pa/ /spyod yul shes pa che nyid shes yangs thob gyur nas/ /de yi rjes la thams cad mkhyen par dbang bskur 'thob/ /
182a4(phal chen): yul yangs ting 'dzin de dag thos pa de/ /gang tshe de yis kun mkhyen dbang bskur thob pa'i tshe/ /pad mo rgya chen rin chen kun gyis brgyan pa 'byung / /de yi tshul 'thun lus kyi dbyings su gnas
182a5(phal chen): par 'gyur/ /rgyal ba'i sras kyis yongs bskor de la lta zhing gnas/ /de yi 'od gzer khrag khrig mtha' yas stong phrag mang / /phyogs bcu'i 'gro ba'i sdug bsngal kun kyang zhi bar byed/ /
182a6(phal chen): mgo yi gtsug nas 'od gzer bye ba stong byung zhing / /phyogs rnams kun gyi mi yi gtso bo'i 'khor du rgyu/ /sting gi nam mkha'i dbyings la 'od gzer dra ba gnas/ /sangs rgyas mchod phyir brtson
182a7(phal chen): par rgyal ba'i zhabs su 'dong / /de'i tshe rgyal ba rnams dang rgyal sra rnams kyis kyang / /chos rab don du rgyal sras dbang bskur 'thob par mkhyen/ /mchod pa'i don du rgyal sras mtha' yas kun kyang 'dong / /
182a8(phal chen): de tshe kun mkhyen dbang bskur mi mchog mdzod spu nas/ /dbang bskur 'od gzer dam pa mang po 'byung bar 'gyur/ /'od gzer mchog gis bskor cing spyi bo'i gtsug tu nub/ /gang tshe rgyal
182b1(phal chen): mchog bu'i thu bo srid mchog la/ /dbang bskur bzhin du sangs rgyas kun gyis dbang bskur tshe/ /phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten thams cad kun nas g.yo bar 'gyur/ /mnar med bar gyi sdug bsngal
182b2(phal chen): zhi zhing nub/ gang tshe kun mkhyen dbang gis mngon par dbang bskur ba/ /de phyir mkhas pas chos sprin sa mchog thob ces bya/ /mkhas pa 'di la gnas pa'i shes rgyud tshad med de/ /sa rab 'di la
182b3(phal chen): gnas pa 'gro kun gtso yin no/ /gzugs dang gzugs med de bzhin 'dod pa'i khams yangs dang / /sems can khams dang zhing dang chos khams yangs pa dang / /grangs dang grangs med nam
182b4(phal chen): mkha'i khams kyi bar du ste/ /chos dbyings yangs pas thams cad ma nor khong du chud/ /'di la mkhas pa mthu chen sprul pa'i las kun dang / /de bzhin byin rlabs rgyal ba'i ye shes phra ba dang / /
182b5(phal chen): mi mchog gsang ba bskal pa'i grangs rnams shes bya dang / /skra rtse gcig tu 'jig rten khams rnams gzud pa dang / /mi yi gtso bo 'byung dang sku tshe 'tshang rgya dang / /'khor lo dam pa bskor dang mya ngan
182b6(phal chen): 'da' ba rnams/ /thams cad rab shes gong du rnam thar zhi ba dag /sngan chad ma thob kun kyang de tshe rab tu 'thob/ /'di la gnas pa'i mthu chen rgyal ba'i chos kyi sprin/ /thams cad khong du
182b7(phal chen): chud byed dran pas kun kyang 'dzin/ /klu rnams kun gyi sprin char rgya mtsho 'dzin pa ltar/ /de bzhin rgyal ba'i chos sprin char chen kun kyang 'dzin/ /rgyal ba gcig las chos gang mthu chen des
182b8(phal chen): thob pa/ /de la phyogs bcu mtha' yas zhing gi sems can rnams/ /thams cad bde gshegs nyan thos 'dzin gyur kyang / /byang chub sems dpa' thos pa'i grangs char nyer mi
183a1(phal chen): 'gro/ /ye shes spyod pa'i stobs kyis sngan cad spyad pa'i mthus/ /skad gcig yud tsam gcig tu khrag khrig zhing bkang zhing / /bdud rtsi'i char 'beb nyon mongs kun kyang zhi
183a2(phal chen): bar byed/ /de phyir rgyal bas 'di ming chos kyi sprin ces gsungs/ /'di nas mthu chen lha'i 'jig rten gtsor gyur pa'i/ /phyogs rnams kun tu mi yi gtso ba'i yul yang ston/ /
183a3(phal chen): rnam 'phrul khrag khrig stong phrag du ma yang ston te/ /byang chub spyod pa de sems 'gro ba mos par byed/ /mkhas pa legs ldan 'di gnas gom pa bor ba tsam/ /sa dgu'i bar du gnas pas shes par mi
183a4(phal chen): nus na/ /sems can gzhan gyis shes par mi 'gyur smos ci dgos/ /dus gsum nyan thos rang rgyal kun gyis de bzhin no/ /'di gnas thams cad mkhyen par 'gro ba kun la ston/ /shes pas
183a5(phal chen): dus gsum kun tu thogs med zhi chos can/ /zhing rnams kun tu rgyas bkang chos rnams kun gyi bar/ /rgyal ba yon tan brjod cing ston pa byed/ /mkhas pa 'di la gnas pa sangs rgyas
183a6(phal chen): mchod byed cing / /phyogs rnams kun tu zhing dang chos kyi dbyings bkang ste/ /rgyal ba mngon du mchod pas mchod byin 'phrog pa med/ /yon tan kun dang ldan pas lha'i lha zhes bya/ /mkhas
183a7(phal chen): pa 'di gnas shes rab snang bas 'gro kun gyis/ /mun pa kun la chos kyi tshul yang rab tu ston/ /dbang phyug dam pa'i mthu yis 'gro ba'i 'dod chags sel/ /de bas rgyal
183a8(phal chen): sras nyon mongs sel la mkhas shes bya/ /'di la gnas pa de dag khams gsum dbang phyug 'gyur/ /ye shes tshul shes theg pa gsum po ston la mkhas/ /skad gcig yud tsam
183b1(phal chen): gcig gis ting 'dzin gcig min thob/ /phyogs bcu kun tu rgyal ba'i dam pa gcig min ston/ /'di ni bdag gis rgyal sras sa rnams mdor bstan gyi/ /rgya cher bskal pa brgya phrag
183b2(phal chen): stong gis bstan mi nus/ /yon tan 'di 'dra'i sangs rgyas ye shes sa 'di la/ /gnas pa rtag tu ri yi rgyal po bzhin myi g.yo/ /rgyal sras thog ma gtsug lag kun gyis mi g.yo ste/ /
183b3(phal chen): sman gyi rnam pa kun nas ri rgyal gang bzhin no/ /tshul khrims thos pas gnyis pa spos ngad spos dang 'dra/ /rnam 'dul me tog ji bzhin gsum pa shes par bya/ /lam la mos bzhin mi 'khrugs 'od
183b4(phal chen): 'phro thob pa ste/ /drang srong gnas bzhin mkhas pa rnams kyi brten gyur pa'i/ /gnod sbyin gnya' shing 'dzin bzhin bsam yas lnga pa thob/ /rta rna'i shing tog 'dra bar drug pa'i 'bras
183b5(phal chen): bu ste/ /bdun pa sa 'dzin klu bzhin shes rab chen pos thob/ /'khor yug dbang ldan bzhin du brgyad pa dbang can thob/ /dgu pa dri ma sel ba dpal can lha min bzhin/ /bcu pa rgyal ba'i
183b6(phal chen): legs ldan ri rab lha gnas 'dra/ /dang po smon lam sngon 'gro gong ma tshul khrims tshogs/ /gsum pa spyod pa'i yon tan bzhi pa gcig gi dngos/ /lnga pa dge mang drug pa shin tu zab
183b7(phal chen): pa'i dngos/ /brgyad pa blo gros yangs pa kun tu gcig min brgyan/ /dgu pa mkhas pa ye shes phra zhing zab dang ldan/ /'gro rgyud thams cad ye shes ldan pas rab tu gnon/ /bcu pa
183b8(phal chen): rgyal ba rnams las yang dag chos 'dzin te/ /rgyal sras spyod pa mi skul rgya mtsho de 'dra'o/ /spyod pa bcu 'das thog ma'i sems rab skye bar 'gyur/ /dka' thub rtul bas gnyis pa
184a1(phal chen): gsum pa bsam gtan gyis/ /dgu pas bzhi pa shin tu byang bas lnga pa'o/ /drug pa rnon pos rtogs pa bdun pa mi phyed pa/ /brgyad pa mthu chen rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan yin/ /
184a2(phal chen): dgu pa ye shes ldan pas thibs po'i spyod pa shes/ /bcu la rgyal bas dbang bskur rgyal po dbang thob bzhin/ /yon tan rin chen dag pas de bzhin rim du 'phar/ /phyogs rnams kun gyi zhing rnams
184a3(phal chen): gzhig ste bgrang bar nus/ /rnam shes gcig gis 'gro ba kun sems shes par rung / /nam mkha'i dbyings kun skra yis gzhal bar nus srid kyi/ /rgyal po yon tan khrag khrig bskal
184a4(phal chen): par bshad mi nus/ /de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis mngon par gnang ste/ yid dga' bar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
184a5(phal chen): rdo rje'i snying pos de skad ces smras pa dang / bcom ldan 'das gzhan 'phrul dbang byed kyi lha'i nang na bzhugs shing mngon par sangs rgyas nas ring por ma lon te/ zhag bdun pa gnyis la
184a6(phal chen): bab pa'i tshe lha'i rgyal po dbang byed kyi gzhal med khang nor bu rin po che'i snying po can na bzhugs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos bshad pa la mngon par dgyes pa mdzad do/ /
184a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor de dag thams cad dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / brgya byin dang tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten mgon dang / dbang phyug chen po dang /

184b1(phal chen): bam po nyi shu gsum pa'o/ /bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi rlabs la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la sogs pa thams cad kyang byang

184b6(phal chen): po de dag thams cad kyang ming 'di zhes bya ba dag ste/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu snang bas mdzod kyi snying pos byung ba zhes bya ba dang / byang chub sems

199a1(phal chen): song ba dang / 'di lta ste/ lhag pa'i bsam pa gtsang mas spyod pa zhes bya ba dang / 'di lta ste 'das pa'i rgyan gyi snying po zhes bya ba dang / 'di lta ste/ ye shes rnam par snang ba'i snying

204b5(phal chen): 'gyur ro/ /de ltar na gcig gis gcig snang bar bya ba'i tshul du ri mtshams de dag tu nyi ma'i gzugs brnyan shar cing rin po che'i ri de dag la nyi ma'i gzugs brnyan 'byung ba de'i phyir rin po che'i

204b7(phal chen): ma yin/ dngos po myed pa 'ang ma yin/ yod pa 'ang ma yin myed pa 'ang ma yin/ ri rnams la gnas pa 'ang ma yin/ nang du phyin pa 'ang ma yin/ phyi rol na gnas pa 'ang ma yin/ de dag dang

205a1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dmigs pa 'jig par yang mi byed do/ /chos rnams kyi rang bzhin yang yongs su myi spong ngo / /byang chub sems dpa' de nyid 'jig rten gyi khams kyi nang

205a7(phal chen): ma gcig dang / nyin zhag bdun dang zla ba phyed dang / zla ba gcig dang zla ba gcig kyang ston to/ /lo gcig kyang ston to/ /lo brgya yang ston to/ /grong yang ston to/ /yul yang ston

210b3(phal chen): kyang de bzhin gshegs pa de dag skye ba'i tshe 'ang mi dmyigs so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe 'ang 'jig par myi dmyigs kyang mtshan yod pas sangs rgyas la sangs rgyas
210b4(phal chen): kyi 'du shes kyis rnam par dmyigs so/ /mtshan ma myed pas mtshan ma myed pa'i mtshan mas myi dmyigs te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi
210b5(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin lhag pa'i bsam pa gtsang mas spyod pa zhes pa ste/ de la snyoms par zhugs shing rnam par langs kyang de ni 'jigs pa myed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di lta ste dper na/
210b6(phal chen): myi gnyid kyis log pa rmi lam rmyis nas sad de mtshan ma yid kyis zin la dran zhing rmi lam la sgrib pa myed pa rnam par dmyigs pa ni sad kyang rmi lam rjes su dran pas yongs su dran no/ /kye rgyal
210b7(phal chen): ba'i sras dag / de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyang sangs rgyas mthong ba'i mtshan ma yang yongs su 'jig par mi byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi chos blangs pa
210b8(phal chen): rnams kyang yang dag par 'dzin to/ /de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gis 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag par yang bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmyigs so/ /sangs rgyas kyi
211a1(phal chen): zhing gi rgyan kyang rjes su 'thob par byed do/ /don gyi tshul yang rnam par 'phel bar byed do/ /chos thams cad kyi tshul yang rnam pa du mar yongs su sbyong ngo / /ye shes kyi sgron me yang
211a2(phal chen): shin tu yangs par byed do/ /sangs rgyas kyi rigs kyang rnam par 'phel bar byed do/ /myi 'jigs pa yongs su dag pa yang rab tu brjod do/ /tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa mi zad pa
211a3(phal chen): 'ang rab tu ston to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi ting nge 'dzin rgya chen po la mkhas pa'i ye shes bzhi pa'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i
211a4(phal chen): sras dag / gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od la rab tu 'jug go/ /bskal pa gcig nas gcig
211a5(phal chen): du brgyud pas/ zhing gcig nas gcig du brgyud pa khong du chud par byed do/ /zhing gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rab tu shes so/ /

211a8(phal chen): 'dul ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rab tu shes so/ /'dul ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sku tshe gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa rab tu shes
211b1(phal chen): so/ /sku tshe gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas/ lo grangs bye ba khrag khrig gcig nas gcig tu shes te/ de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes mtha' yas pa 'dab chags
211b2(phal chen): par rab tu shes so/ /de bzhin du 'das pa'i zhing rnam 'dab chags par rab tu shes so/ /de bzhin du 'das pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs rnams 'dab chags par rab tu shes so/ /

211b6(phal chen): so/ /de bzhin du 'das pa'i rnam par byang ba rnam par dag pa rnams 'dab chags par rab tu shes so/ /de dag ting nge 'dzin 'das pa rnam par dag pa'i snying po zhes bya ba la snyoms
211b7(phal chen): par 'jug ste/ sems bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa brgya phrag stong la 'jug go/ /de dang 'dab chags pa'i sems mtha' yas pas bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya phrag
211b8(phal chen): stong la 'jug go/ /bskal pa tshad myed pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa dpag tu med pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa gzhal du med pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa mu med pa la 'jug go/ /
212a1(phal chen): bskal pa sa mtshams myed pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa grangs myed pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa la 'jug go/ /bskal pa dpag gis mi khyab pa la 'jug go/ /
212a2(phal chen): bskal pa brjod du myid pa'i yang brjod du med pa la 'jug go/ /de dag ting nge 'dzin da ltar byung ba'i 'gag pa myed pa la 'das pa ma skyes shing sgrib pa myed pa zhes bya ba la snyoms par 'jug te/
212a3(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin de dag chos bcus dbang bskur ba yin/ de dag de las langs nas kyang de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la dbang bskur ba'i chos bcu po de dag la bsam kyis mi khyab par yang

212b4(phal chen): mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku stong gi 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du rab tu mthong ngo / /de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku stong gnyis kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du rab tu mthong ngo / /

213b1(phal chen): yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de rnam par 'phel bar yang mi byed/ 'grib par yang myi byed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di lta ste dper na/ nam mkha' ni yung dkar srin bus zos pa'i

213b8(phal chen): can rnams kyi 'chi 'pho dang skye ba ni sems la gsol ba gdab pa myed do/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin 'di dag la gnas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan dang sangs rgyas
214a1(phal chen): rnam par dmyigs pa yang nan tan bya myi dgos par rnam par dag ste/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni myur ba bcu dang ldan pa yin/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ spyod pa la yang dag par byung
214a2(phal chen): bas yongs su rdzogs par bya ba myur du yongs su rdzogs par byed pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi chos snang bas 'jig rten myur du snang bar byed pa yin/ chos kyi 'khor lo'i thabs mkhas pas sems

214a5(phal chen): sems can thams cad myur du tshim par byed pa yin/ mos pa dang 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin rnam par 'phrul ba myur du yang dag par ston pa yin/ 'jig rten thams cad du sgra skad sna tshogs

214b3(phal chen): dgang sla ba yin/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni don shes shing 'gro ba thams cad yongs su 'dul bar byed pa'i phyir rgyun 'chad pa myed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni don shes shing mkhas par bya ba la shin tu

214b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos thams cad la slob dpon myed pa yin/ 'gro ba thams cad du 'gro ba'i rtsal yod pas gzhan gyi dring myi 'jog pa yin/ sems rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal zhing dag pa dang ldan pas
214b7(phal chen): shin tu dag pa yin/ 'jig rten thams cad yongs su 'dren pa la zhugs pas thu bo dam pa yin/ skye dgu thams cad la bsam pa thag pa nas phan pa yin/ ma 'ongs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rigs
214b8(phal chen): rab tu bsgrub pa yin/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo la rab tu gzhog pa yin/ gnyis su myed par smra zhing nor ba myed par khong du chud par ston pas de kho na nyid la mkhas pa yin/ sangs rgyas
215a1(phal chen): kyi chos thams cad kyi chos kyi mdzod rab tu gtang ba yin/ sems can gyi ris rnams su bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi sprin gyi char 'bebs pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /
215a2(phal chen): 'di lta ste dper na/ brgya byin mngon par dga' ba'i nor bu rin po che ni/ lha'i rgyal po'i spyi bo la btags na/ nor bu de'i byin gyis lha'i dbang po brgya byin 'od dang ldan par gyur pa ste/ nor bu rin
215a3(phal chen): po che bdag pos lha'i rgyal po brgya byin chos bcus sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i lha thams cad zil gyi gnon te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sum bcu rtsa gsum rigs kyi lha'i bu gzhan thams cad kyi lha rdzas

215a6(phal chen): las 'das pa'i shes rab ste/ de ni lha rdzas las 'das pa'i bsod nams rab tu grub pas nor bu rin po che de thob pa'i phyir ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de bzhin du byang chub sems
215a7(phal chen): dpa' de yang ting nge 'dzin 'di thob pas ye shes kyi tshogs chen po yangs pa'i gter chen po bcu 'thob po/ /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad snang bar bya ba'i
215a8(phal chen): ye shes rab tu thob po/ /'di lta ste sems can gyi khams thams cad du skye zhing 'byung ba'i ye shes rab tu thob po/ /'di lta ste/ dus gsum du sprul pa'i byin gyis rlabs pa'i ye shes

215b4(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ chos 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par khong du chud pa rab tu thob bo/ /ting nge 'dzin 'di thob ma thag tu byang chub sems dpa' de rnam par dmyigs pa thams cad 'jig rten gyi

215b6(phal chen): phyir/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa rab tu 'gyed do/ /'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir/ kha dog du ma dang / kha dog sna tshogs
215b7(phal chen): dang / 'od kyi 'khor brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed par byin gyis brlob po/ /'di lta ste/ sems can byin gyis brlab cing 'dul ba'i phyir 'od gzer kyi dkyil 'khor brjod du myed
215b8(phal chen): pa'i yang brjod du myed pa rab tu 'gyed do/ /'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi spyan sngar 'gro ba'i phyir lus brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed par byin gyis rlob po/ /'di lta ste/
216a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkur ba'i phyir/ spos dang mye tog sna tshogs yid du 'ong ba'i sprin du ma brjod du myed pa yang brjod du myed pa'i char mngon par 'bebs so/ /'di lta
216a2(phal chen): ste sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba dang / sems can 'dul ba'i phyir ba spu'i khung bu re rer yang rol mo brdung ba dang dkral ba dang brgya phrag du ma yid du 'ong zhing rgya che ba brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du
216a3(phal chen): myed pa byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste sems can mos pa'i tshul bzhin yongs su smyin par bya ba'i phyir/ sprul pa'i rgyud rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pa dang / khyu mchog gi mthu dang
216a4(phal chen): rnam par sprul pa'i sprul pa du ma brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa la rab tu rten to/ /'di lta ste phyogs bcur sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa tha dad pa sna tshogs yongs su dri ba'i phyir gom pa
216a5(phal chen): re res 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa yongs su 'da' bar byed do/ /'di lta ste/ mthong ba dang / thos pa dang / mchod pa thams cad don yod par bya ba'i
216a6(phal chen): phyir spyi gtsug bltar myi snang ba'i lus rnam par dag pa dang / gzugs dang mtshan sna tshogs rnam par dag pa brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa rab tu 'thob bo/ /'di lta ste sgra skad sna
216a7(phal chen): tshogs dang / sgra skad du mas 'gro ba rnams rnam par bstan pa'i phyir/ sgra dang skad dang / nga ro dang dbyangs kyi yan lag brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa rab tu brjod do/ /de ltar byang chub sems
216a8(phal chen): dpa' lus kyi gzi brjid phun sum tshogs shing / rnam par dag pa bcu rab tu thob po/ /byang chub sems dpa' de ni sems can byin gyis brlab pa yongs su rdzogs par bya ba bcu rab tu thob
216b1(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas mthong zhing rnam par dmyigs par bya ba'i phyir/ sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas la dad pa rab tu 'thob par bya
216b2(phal chen): ba'i phyir/ sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste chos nyan cing khong du chud par bya ba'i phyir sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas dang bcas pa'i 'jig
216b3(phal chen): rten gyi khams bstan pa'i phyir/ sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /
216b4(phal chen): 'di lta ste las ji ltar bsags pa bzhin du dran par bya ba'i phyir sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste rtse gcig tu 'gyur ba yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir sems can byin gyis
216b5(phal chen): rlob bo/ /'di lta ste sangs rgyas kyi cha byad rnam par dag par bya ba'i phyir sems can rnams la byin gyis rlob bo/ /'di lta ste/ byang chub kyi sems la 'jug par bya ba'i phyir sems can
216b6(phal chen): rnams byin gyi rlob bo/ /'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir sems can rnams byin gyis rlob bo/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de ltar byang chub sems dpa'
216b7(phal chen): de ni sems can byin gyis brlab pa bcus yongs su rdzogs par byed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems can byin gyis brlab pa bcu yongs su rdzogs par
216b8(phal chen): byas nas sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bcu byed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' ni thos pas kyang sems can rnams yongs su smyin par byed pas
217a1(phal chen): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' ni mthong bas kyang sems can 'dul ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed
217a2(phal chen): pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' ni rjes su dran pas kyang sems rnam par dag par 'gyur bas sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' ni 'jig rten gyi khams
217a3(phal chen): skyod pas kyang ngan song gsum rnam par bzlog pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' ni byin gyis rlabs kyis kyang sems can rnams kyi dran pa nyams par myi 'gyur
217a4(phal chen): ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa' ni rmyi lam du mthong bas kyang sems can rnams kyi dran pa nyams par myi 'gyur ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa

217a6(phal chen): ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang dag par ston pas kyang sems can smon lam bsam gyis mi khyab pa la rab tu gzhog pas sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin/ byang chub sems dpa'

217a8(phal chen): pas kyang sems can mi dga' ba ldan pas shin tu rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byed pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' sems
217b1(phal chen): can la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bcu byed do/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de ting nge 'dzin chen po lus yang dag par 'dres pa zhes bya

217b3(phal chen): gnas pa dang / phyogs thams cad la myi gnas pa dang / bskal pa thams cad la mi gnas pa dang / sems can thams cad la myi gnas pa dang / chos thams cad la myi gnas

251a1(phal chen): dang snyoms par 'jug pa kun tu bzang po'i spyod yul la yang dag par gnas pa'i rnam pa de lta bu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul la rmongs pa myed cing chos thams cad la
251a2(phal chen): rab tu gzhol bar bya ba'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i blo gros nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yang dag par gzhol zhing chos rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad kyi don khong
251a3(phal chen): du chud par bya'o/ /phyir blo gros nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad de/ chags pa myed pa la rtogs par bzhog pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongs su 'dzin par bya ba'i phyir rig pa nye bar
251a4(phal chen): bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /ye shes 'byam klas pa khong du chud par bya ba dang / blos rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i chos dbyings kyi yul gyi mtha' klas pa thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi byang chub
251a5(phal chen): nye bar bsgrub par mdzad do/ /byang chub sems dpa' de chos kyi snang ba dang / 'od thams cad kyis mun pa myed pa'i ye shes 'byam klas pa las phyir myi ldog par bya ba'i phyir shes rab
251a6(phal chen): nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /byang chub sems dpa' de thabs mkhas pa 'jig rten thams cad las 'phags pas sems can 'dul ba la bsgrib pa myed par bya ba'i phyir ye shes nye bar
251a7(phal chen): bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /byang chub sems dpa' de chos kyi rgyud mtha' yas pa brjod pa la zad myi shes pa tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa skyod pa'i phyir spobs pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /byang
251a8(phal chen): c hub sems dpa' de 'gro ba thams cad du lus brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa'i rgyu de dang kha dog mtha' yas pa rnam pa tha dad pa rnam par ston par bya ba'i phyir sprul pa nye bar bsgrub
251b1(phal chen): pa mdzad do/ /byang chub sems dpa' de sems can sna tshogs thams cad la dbyangs kyi yan lag dang ldan pa'i sgra dbyangs dang skad sna tshogs bstan par bya ba'i phyir lce yangs pa nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /
251b2(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de mthong ma thag tu ston pa dang / thos par byas pas sems can thams cad la yongs su smyin par bya ba la rmongs pa myed par bya ba phyir nye bar bsgrub pa mdzad do/ /
251b3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la yongs su grub pa yin/ yongs su grub nas yang thams cad mkhyen pa'i sgo yongs su rdzogs par bya bas de bzhin
251b4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i rigs la 'jug go/ /'byung ba'i sgo yongs su dag par byed do/ /chags pa myed pa'i sgos yongs su 'byung bar byed do/ /sems can thams cad 'byung ba'i sgo yongs su brtsom
251b5(phal chen): zhing byin gyi brlobs po/ /chos thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i sgo yang dag par ston to/ /cho 'phrul gyi sgo tshad myed pas sems can 'dul ba la rab tu 'jug go/ /byang chub sems dpa'
251b6(phal chen): kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i rnam pa la rab tu mkhas par sbyong ngo / /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba la byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pas yang dag par 'byung
251b7(phal chen): ngo / /phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i 'gro ba thams cad gdul ba'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rnam par phye ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'gro ba thams cad gdul ba'i mthar
251b8(phal chen): thug par byin gyis brlabs kyi byin tu rlob po/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni smon lam gyi khyad par de lta bu dang ldan pas yongs su grub par grub na/ 'jig rten thams
252a1(phal chen): cad kyi slob dpon du gyur pa yin/ chos kyi nyi ma 'jig rten du shar ba yin/ ye shes kyi bla ma 'jig rten thams cad du snang bar byung ba yin/ ye shes dam pa'i ri rab myi g.yo ba 'jig
252a2(phal chen): rten thams cad las mngon par 'phags pa yin/ ye shes kyi rgya mtsho tshad myed pa 'jig rten thams cad du yang dag par gnas pa yin/ bsgrub pa rgyun myi chad pas 'jig rten thams cad du
252a3(phal chen): chos kyi nan tan byed pa yin/ 'jig rten gyi khams sa mtshams myed pa thams cad du rab tu snang ba yin/ rnam par dag pa yangs shing mtha' yas pa 'gro ba thams cad du brjod pa yin/
252a4(phal chen): sems can gyi khams mtha' dang dbus myed pa dge ba'i rtsa ba dang bsod nams kyi rgyud dang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa'i smon lam chen po rab tu brtson par gzhog pa yin/ kun
252a5(phal chen): tu bzang pos spyod pa'i brtson 'grus yangs pa rgya chen po'i smon lam chen po la rab tu gzhog pa yin/ spyod pa chen po dang ting nge 'dzin yangs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa brjod du myed pa'i yang
252a6(phal chen): brjod du myed pa la sems can gyi khams yang dag par gzhog cing rab tu sbyor ro/ /de ltar byang chub sems dpa' de lta bu'i ngang tshul can de lta bu'i ye shes can/ de lta bu'i chos thob par
252a7(phal chen): gyur pa/ de lta bu'i chos kyi snang bar gyur pa/ de lta bu'i chos la gnas pa/ chos de lta bu mthong bar gyur pa/ mngon par shes pa de lta bu'i yid dang ldan pa/ cho 'phrul dam pa de lta bu
252a8(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ cho 'phrul mchog tu bya ba phul du byung ba de lta bus yang dag par bsgrub pa/ rtag tu brtson pa'i snying rje chen pos mngon par 'phags pa/ chos kyi don bzang po la rtag tu rgyun
252b1(phal chen): myi 'chad par brtson pa/ bde ba'i lam yang dag par ston pa/ bsod nams chen po dang ye shes yangs pa'i 'od zer gyi rgyal mtshan du gyur pa/ rnam par thar pa bsam gyis myi khyab pa shin tu
252b2(phal chen): thob pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul la don yod par rjes su song ba/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa/ rnam par thar pa'i tshul shin tu phra ba/ bsam gyis mi khyab
252b3(phal chen): pa rab tu sgoms pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyud dang / tshul rmongs pa myed par khong du chud pa/ kun tu bzang po'i ting nge 'dzin brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa la rnam par brtse zhing brjod
252b4(phal chen): pa/ sing ge bsgyings pa'i ye shes kyis grub pa la shin tu gnas pa/ sems dang yid rnam par shes pa la chags pa myed pa rnams kyi chos kyi bsam pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa rab tu
252b5(phal chen): yangs pa chen po bcu 'byung ngo / /bcu gang zhe na/ 'di la byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas thams cad rjes su dran pas gnas pa yin/ chos thams cad kyi de bzhin nyid tshad myed
252b6(phal chen): pa la gnas pa yin/ sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i snying rje chen pos gnas pa yin/ zhing rnam par dag pa'i gnas bsam gyis myi khyab pa'i phyir gnas pa rnam par dag pas gnas pa
252b7(phal chen): yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yul la mos pa rnam par dag pas gnas pa yin/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub tha dad
252b8(phal chen): par myi byed pas gnas pa yin/ chags pa myed pa'i mtha' sgrib pa med pa'i chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dang / rang bzhin mtshan nyid myed pas gnas pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa
253a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba thams cad dang rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur pas gnas pa yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
253a2(phal chen): kyi sku'i phrin las dang gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi phrin las 'das pa dang ma byung ba dang / da ltar byung ba myed pa'i chos kyi dbyings shin tu ston pa'i ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'i gnas pa
253a3(phal chen): yin/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba thams cad kyi skye ba dang / mngon par 'byung ba dang / snying po byang chub tu gshegs pa dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya ba dang /
253a4(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba dus rnam pa nyid du thugs su chud pa/ skad cig gcig gi mthar 'jug pa yin te/ de ltar byang chub sems dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam
253a5(phal chen): pa de dag ni tshad myed pa/ shin tu yangs pa bgrang du myed pa gzhal du myed pa/ zad mi shes pa brjod par dka' ba/ bsam gyi mi khyab pa brjod du myed pa/ bzod par dka' ba/ 'gro ba thams
253a6(phal chen): cad kyis myi 'phrogs pa dag ste/ chos thams cad kyi ye shes rab tu bsgrub pa'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' de dag lhag pa'i bsam pa de lta bus gnas so/ /de dag gi byang chub sems dpa'
253a7(phal chen): de byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa yin te/ chos rnam par dag par yang rab tu thob bo/ /bsam pa'i stobs kyang rnam par 'phel bar byed do/ /sems
253a8(phal chen): can rnams la dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad myed pa yang yang dag par ston to/ /byang chub sems dpa'i stobs kyang rnam par 'phel bar byed do/ /byang chub sems dpa'i yon tan gyi mi khom pa khom par
253b1(phal chen): byed pa thams cad kyang yongs su rdzogs par byed do/ /shin tu 'byung ba'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad yongs su grub pa yang rab tu thob po/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi
253b2(phal chen): bzungs kyi 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bstan pa yang dag par 'dzin to/ /'dod chags dang bral ba'i mthar sems can gyi khams thams cad la yang dag
253b3(phal chen): par blta'o/ /tshig gi lam gyis rgyud kyi sems can thams cad 'dul ba yongs su ston to/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni ting nge 'dzin rgya chen po de lta bu thob pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos
253b4(phal chen): nyid de/ des byang chub sems dpa' de sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'byam klas pa thams cad la mchog tu bya bar rab tu thob po/ /de'i phyir chos 'byam klas pa thams cad ston pa la mkhas pa'i tha
253b5(phal chen): dad pa yang dag par shes pa rab tu thob bo/ /de'i phyir 'jig rten thams cad du chos kyi dam pa 'jigs pa myed pa rnam par dag pa rab tu thob po/ /de'i phyir ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi rjes su 'gro
253b6(phal chen): ba'i ye shes rab tu thob po/ /de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa'i tshul thams cad la mkhas pa'i dam par rab tu thob po/ /de'i phyir tshul thams cad kyi rgyan rab tu thob po/ /de'i phyir 'jig rten
253b7(phal chen): thams cad du chos kyi dbugs phyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa dang ldan par 'gyur ro/ /de'i phyir sems can thams cad kyi dus dang dus ma yin pa rab tu shes so/ /de'i phyir 'jig rten gyis khams
253b8(phal chen): thams cad snang bar bya ba rab tu shes so/ /de'i phyir sems can thams cad la sgrib pa myed pa'i ye shes khong du chud par 'gyur ro/ /de'i phyir don thams cad bsgrub par yon tan thams cad
254a1(phal chen): la yan lag rab tu gnas par 'gyur ro/ /de'i phyir theg pa'i dam pa rab tu brtson par byas te/ sems can thams cad la mnyam par gzhag pa rnam par dag pa rab tu brjod do/ /de
254a2(phal chen): ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi don la gnas pa snying rje chen po de lta bu rnam par 'phel bar byed pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten par 'dod pa/ sangs rgyas thams
254a3(phal chen): cad blta bar 'dod pa/ chos thams cad snang bar bya bar 'dod pa/ zhing thams cad tu 'gro bar 'dod pas bgrod pa/ phyogs thams cad du rgyu bar 'dod pa/ dus gsum mnyam pa nyid khong du chud
254a4(phal chen): par 'dod pa/ chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pa/ sangs rgyas mnyam pa nyid la rab tu gnas par 'dod pa/ ye shes mnyam pa nyid la 'dus par 'dod pas
254a5(phal chen): chos 'di dag la las de lta bur brtson zhing las gzhan myed pa dang / don shes pa dang / sems ma 'khrugs pa dang / yid rtse gcig tu gyur pa dang / de ltar gnas pa la brtson pa dang / de ltar
254a6(phal chen): khong du chud pa'i yid dang / de ltar mnyam pa'i sems dang / de lta bu'i yid bde ba dang / de ltar las su rung ba dang / de ltar brtson pa dang / de ltar mthar 'byin pa dang / de ltar rnam par spyod
254a7(phal chen): pa dang / nan tan du bya zhing mngon par bsgrub par bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni legs par smra ba yin/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni gzhan du smra ba ma yin
254a8(phal chen): te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni ji skad du smras pa de bzhin du byed pa'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta ste dper na/ rdo rje gcig tu myi rung bar rjod pa ste/ myi tshogs pa'i rang bzhin yongs su
254b1(phal chen): mi stong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang chos 'di dag las brjod pa ste 'di lta bu'i chos la gnas pa yongs su mi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ gser ni kha dog shin tu bzang bar brjod
254b2(phal chen): pa ste/ gser gyi kha dog bzang pos rnam par dag pa yongs su myi gtong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang de ltar dge zhing bzang ba'i chos kyis brjod pa ste/ de ltar dge zhing bzang po'i
254b3(phal chen): chos la gnas pa yongs su mi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ lha'i bu nyi ma ni snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyis brjod pa ste/ snang ba yongs su myi gtong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'gro
254b4(phal chen): ba thams cad du snang bas brjod pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i snang ba yongs su myi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ ri'i rgyal po ri rab ni rin po che bzhi'i phung po rgya mtsho las shin tu 'phags
254b5(phal chen): par brjod pa ste/ rgya mtsho las 'phags pa yongs su myi gtong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'jig rten thams cad la dge ba'i rtsa bas shin tu 'phags par brjod pa ste/ 'jig
254b6(phal chen): rten thams cad las shin tu 'phags pa yongs su mi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ sa chen po ni 'gro ba thams cad yongs su ston par brjod pa ste/ rten pa'i rang bzhin yongs su myi gtong
254b7(phal chen): ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang 'gro ba thams cad yongs su 'grel pas brjod pa ste/ snying rje chen po yongs su myi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ rgya mtsho chen po ni rin po che
254b8(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su brjod pa ste/ rgya mtsho'i chu yongs su myi gtong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su brjod pa ste/ sems
255a1(phal chen): can thams cad yongs su dgrol ba'i smon lam yongs su myi gtong ngo / /'di lta ste dper na/ 'phong gi slob dpon ni mda' gzhu dang 'phong la zo bdog bde bas ji srid du mda' gzhu
255a2(phal chen): dang ldan zhing mda' gzhu la brtson pas brjod par bya ste/ 'phong gi tshul du bya ba yongs su mi gtong ngo / /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ji tsam du ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo dang / yul gyi rnam pa
255a3(phal chen): 'di lta bu la mngon par brtson zhing yongs su bsgrub pa de tsam du thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyis snang bar 'gyur ba yin/ 'di lta ste dper na/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po ni ji tsam du tshe ring
255a4(phal chen): ba de tsam du bde ba yod pa yin/ de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ji tsam du byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod cing rnam pa 'di lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin chen po la snyoms par 'jug pa de tsam du
255a5(phal chen): sems can gyi khams rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ /shin tu rnam par dag pa yang dag par thob bo/ /'di lta ste dper na/ ji tsam du sa bon btab pa de tsam du rnam par 'phel lo/ /de bzhin du byang
255a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' yang ci tsam du byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa la brtson pa de tsam du sems can gyi khams rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba la rnam par dag par 'gyur ro/ /'di lta ste dper
255a7(phal chen): na/ sprin chen po ni ji tsam du char 'beb pa de tsam du dbyar gyi dus la sa bon rnam par 'phel bar 'gyur ro/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' yang ji tsam du chos kyi sprin gyi char 'bebs shing
255a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa dang / rnam pa 'di lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin chen po la snyoms par 'jug pa de tsam du sems can rnams shin tu rnam par dag par 'gyur te/ shin tu mthar
255b1(phal chen): thug par 'gyur ba dang / shin tu bde ba phun sum ldan pa dang / mchog tu bya ba shin tu 'thob pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad shin tu tshim par byed pa dang / skye dgu
255b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi bya ba thams cad la the tsom shin tu gom pa dang / sbyin sregs yongs su spyod pas bsod nams rmad du byung ba dang / phyir myi ldog pa'i 'khor lo la rab tu gzhog pa'i
255b3(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du skal ba shin tu mnyam par 'gyur ba dang / sems can thams cad khams gsum las bsgral ba'i phyir ye shes shin tu rnam par dag par byed pa yin/ thams cad
255b4(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes la sems can rnams dgod pa'i phyir chos kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba dam par 'gyur ba yin/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni rang bzhin gyi chos kyi dbyings rnam par phye
255b5(phal chen): ba ste/ bsam gyis myi khyab pa'o/ /tshad myed pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rnam par spyod pa'o/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi phyir ye shes sbyong ba'o/ /yongs su 'dul bas sems can
255b6(phal chen): sbyong ba'o/ /yongs su bsngo bas zhing sbyong ba'o/ /rab tu gzhog pas chos sbyong ba'o/ /zhum pa myed pas mi 'jigs pa sbyong ba'o/ /rab tu bstan pa tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa sbyong ba'o/ /shin tu
255b7(phal chen): bstan pas chos sbyong ba'o/ /chos thams cad las phyir myi ldog par gzungs sbyong ba'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi 'byung ba thams cad kyi don du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa sbyong ba'o/ /de ltar byang chub
255b8(phal chen): sems dpa' ting nge 'dzin 'di la gnas pa ni yon tan 'di dag dang / gzhan yang yongs su dag pa brjod du myed pa'i yang brjod du myed pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong rab tu thob po/ /ting nge 'dzin chen
256a1(phal chen): po'i dkyil 'khor 'di dag gi dbang dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs dang / rang gi dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyu'i stobs dang / ye shes kyi sas sgrol ba'i mthu dang / dge
256a2(phal chen): ba'i bshes gnyen gyis nye bar brten pa'i stobs dang / bdud kyi las thams cad rab tu 'joms pa'i mthu dang / dge ba'i las skal pa mnyam pa rnams kyi gzhung gcig pa'i mthu dang smon lam
256a3(phal chen): rnams kyi dag pa'i stobs dang / ji ltar bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams yongs su bsgrub pa'i stobs dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bsod nams thub pa myed cing zad myi shes pa'i mthu de
256a4(phal chen): ltar snyoms par 'jug pa la gnas pa ni/ yon tan mtshungs pa mnyam pa bcus sangs rgyas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i thams cad mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin te/ bcu
256a5(phal chen): gang zhe na/ 'di ltar gzugs dang mtshan dang dpe byad bzang pos sna tshogs kyi byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ 'od dang 'od zer gyis dra ba rab tu 'gyed pa rnam par dag
256a6(phal chen): pas byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ rdzu 'phrul dang rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sprul pa sems can 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs
256a7(phal chen): pa mnyam pa yin/ lus tshad myed pa dang / kha dog mtha' yas pa dang / dbyangs thams cad rnam par dag pas/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam
256a8(phal chen): par dag pa byin gyis brlob cing sems can gyi las dang spyod pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmyigs pa yang dag par ston pas byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ sems can
256b1(phal chen): thams cad kyi tha snyad gzungs dam pa'i 'dzin pa'i mthu dang dran pa nyams pa myed pa'i mthar thug par gnas par byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ tha dad pa yang dag par shes
256b2(phal chen): pa myi zad pas sems can thams cad kyi sgra skad shes pas/ ston cing chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ myi 'jigs pas bag tsha ba myed par
256b3(phal chen): seng ge'i nga ro sgrog cing chos dang mthun par sems can khong du chud par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ dus gsum gyi tshig lam la 'jug pa skad cig gi mthar
256b4(phal chen): 'jug par byed pas byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa mnyam pa yin/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul rnam par phye ba sems can rnams la yang dag par ston pas/

278b8(phal chen): sems dpa' chen po yang rang gi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gzhan gyi rgyud kyi yul du snang bar byed kyang 'di ni gzhan gyi rgyud do/ /'di ni bdag gi ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor to/ /zhes gnyis
279a1(phal chen): su mi byed do/ /bdag gi yul dang gzhan gyi yul rnam par dbye ba 'ang rab tu shes so/ /'di lta ste dper na sa bon du gyur pa ni shin tu 'phel zhing skye ba yin te/ chu ba dang lo ma dang / sbu
279a2(phal chen): gu'i gnas su gyur pa nas rnam par dbye ba 'ang yod do/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang chos nyid mi gnyis pa la gnyis kyi mtshan nyid mi 'thun pa'i ye shes la
279a3(phal chen): chags pa myed pa'i mtha'i tshul gyis rab tu 'jug go/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi gzugs brnyan lta bu'i bzod pa thob pa ste/

279a6(phal chen): kyi dkyil 'khor gzugs brnyan du gyur pa yang kun tu rnam par dmigs par byed do/ /rjes su song ba'i lus kyang 'jig rten thams cad du phyin par byed do/ /lus rnam par dbye ba chags
279a7(phal chen): pa myed pas spyod pa yang rab tu shes so/ /gang yang 'jig rten na 'jig rten gyi mtshan ma dang / 'jig rten ngang skam yod pa de dag 'dres pa 'ang ma yin/ tha dad pa yang ma yin par rab tu shes
279a8(phal chen): so/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su rigs dang ldan par byung ba'i lus dang ngag dang yid rnam par dag pa 'ang rab tu 'thob po/ /kha dog mtha' yas pa'i lus thams cad rnam par dag pa

279b2(phal chen): dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'jig rten thams cad sprul pa lta bur rab tu 'jug ste/ sems can thams cad kyi bsam pas sprul pa dang / bsams te sprul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
279b3(phal chen): mngon par 'du byed pas sprul pa dang / rnam par rtog pas sprul pa dang / bde ba dang sdug bsngal thams cad kyi phyin ci log gis sprul pa dang / sgro btags pas sprul pa dang / 'jig rten
279b4(phal chen): gyi chos thams cad myed pas sprul pa dang / tshig gi lam gyis byin gyis brlabs kyi sprul pa dang / nyon mongs pa thams cad kyi yongs su rtog pas sprul pa dang / 'du shes kyi sprul pa dang / 'di
279b5(phal chen): lta ste 'dul ba rnam par byang bar bya ba dang / rnam par dag par bya ba'i yongs su rtogs pas sprul pa dang / 'di lta ste dus gsum du phyir myi ldog pas sprul pa mnyam pa nyid kyi byung ba myed pa dang /

279b7(phal chen): rnam par bkod pa dang / 'di lta ste chos kyi 'khor lo dang / thabs mkhas pa'i ye shes kyi sprul pa mi 'jigs pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa'i ye shes kyis 'jug pa rab tu shes te de

280a1(phal chen): par byed do/ /mtha' dang dbus dang mu myed par ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin du thob par byed do/ /grub par byed do/ /dbang du byed do/ /de kho na nyid du shes so/ /yang dag pa nyid las myi g.yo bar byed do/ /

281a1(phal chen): thams cad la rnam par rtog pa myed par spyod pa dang / ji ltar sprul pa de sangs rgyas kyi byang chub dang byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la dub pa myed par spyod pa dang / ji ltar

281b8(phal chen): myed do/ /skye ba yang myed do/ /'di lta ste dper na nam mkha' ni gzhi myed de tha dad pa myed do/ /de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po yang chos thams cad shes pas gzhi myed

301a7(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /shar lho'i phyogs mtshams logs na sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i ri mchod rten zhes bya ba yod de/ de la byang chub sems dpa' lha'i phung po zhes bya ba
301a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor stong dang ldan pa chos ston to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /lho dang nub gyis phyogs mtshams logs na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i ri 'od
301b1(phal chen): ces bya ba yod de/ de la byang chub sems dpa' bzang po'i dpal zhes bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor stong phrag gsum dang ldan pa chos ston to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /nub phyogs
301b2(phal chen): mtshams logs na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i ri spos kyi ngad can zhes bya ba yod de/ de la byang chub sems dpa' spos kyi 'od zer rab tu 'gyed pa zhes bya ba byang chub sems
301b3(phal chen): dpa'i 'khor stong phrag lnga dang ldan pa chos ston to/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /rgya mtsho chen po'i nang na sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas phugs bzang po zhes bya ba yod do/ /
301b4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras dag /yul shin tu yangs pa'i lho phyogs logs na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas rtsa ba shin tu brtan pa/ zhes bya ba yod do/ /yul pa ta la'i bu zhes
301b5(phal chen): bya ba na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun gyi kun dga' ra ba gser gyi gling zhes bya ba yod do/ /yul ma du ra na sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i
301b6(phal chen): gnas tshim par byed pa'i phug ces bya ba yod do/ /yul ril ba gtong zhes bya ba na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas chos kyi bstan zhes bya ba yod do/ /yul dge ba'i phul
301b7(phal chen): du phyin pa zhes bya ba na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas btang bzung gi phug ces bya ba yod do/ /yul be'u ra zhes bya ba na sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs
301b8(phal chen): bzhugs pa'i gnas mthu bo zhes bya ba klu bcug pa yod do/ /yul kam po tsa na sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas/ byams pas 'phags pa zhes bya ba
302a1(phal chen): yod do/ /rgyal ba'i gnas na sngon/ byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i/ gnas mthu bo che'i phug pa ces bya ba yod do/ /yul kha sha na sngon/ byang chub
302a2(phal chen): sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas ba lang gi mgo bo zhes bya ba yod do/ /kha che'i yul na sngon/ byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas shin tu
302a3(phal chen): bstan pa zhes bya ba yod do/ /yul dga' ba 'phel ba zhes bya ba na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas brtan gyis phug ces bya ba yod do/ /yul
302a4(phal chen): chu 'dzin ces bya ba na sngon/ byang chub sems dpa' bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas khyor po ston pa zhes bya ba yod do/ /yul sa 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor na/ sngon byang chub sems dpa'
302a5(phal chen): bzhugs bzhugs pa'i gnas brgyags kyi phug ces bya ba yod do/ /shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo/ /sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ byang chub
